Draft Implementing Rules for the Income Tax (Continued from Yesterday)

Article 20: Those who withhold income tax or pay income tax themselves shall declare the amount of income to the local competent tax collection agency within the period stipulated in Articles 8 to 11 of the Provisional Regulations.

Article 21: The amount of income of a person without capacity for conduct or a person with limited capacity for conduct shall be declared on their behalf by their legal representative in accordance with the provisions of the preceding article.

Article 22: If the profit-making enterprises of Category 1, Items A and B, still have income after being merged, dissolved, closed down, liquidated, and settled, they shall declare the amount of income to the local tax collection agency within 20 days from the date of settlement. If the bankrupt is declared bankrupt and still has income after liquidation, the bankruptcy administrator shall declare the amount of income in accordance with the provisions of the preceding paragraph.

Article 23: When the business year is changed, the person in charge of performing the business shall declare the amount of income within 20 days from the date of settlement in accordance with the provisions of Article 8 of these Detailed Rules.

Article 24: The declarant of Category 1 income shall submit a property list, profit and loss statement, balance sheet, or other account books and documents sufficient to prove the amount of income at the time of declaration.

Article 25: Income tax shall be collected by the competent tax collection agency of the Ministry of Finance, entrusted to the National Bank or the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau. If there is no such agency in the local area, other banks, commercial firms, or places may be designated to collect it on its behalf.

Article 26: The tax payment period for each category of income tax shall be as follows: (1) The tax payment period for Category 1, Items A and B shall be from March 1 to the end of May, or from August 1 to the end of October each year, and shall be paid in one lump sum. The income tax for Item C shall be paid on the date of settlement and declaration. (2) The income tax for Category 2 shall be paid on a monthly basis. (3) The income tax for Category 3 shall be paid at the time of settlement and interest declaration. For Category 1, Item B, Category 2 self-paid income tax and Article 2, Paragraph 1, Paragraph 23 of these Detailed Rules, the income tax payable shall be paid within 20 days from the date of settlement and declaration.

Article 27: The method of paying income tax is as follows: (1) Those belonging to Category 1, Items A and B shall be paid by the person in charge of the business himself. (2) Those belonging to Category 2, Item C shall be withheld by the person in charge of the agency paying the income if there is an agency paying the income. If there is no paying agency, the taxpayer or his agent shall pay it himself. (3) Those belonging to Category 2 shall be withheld by the head of the agency or the employer who directly pays the salary or remuneration. If there is no paying agency or employer, they shall pay it themselves. (4) Those belonging to Category 3 shall be withheld by the person in charge of the interest-paying agency.

Article 28: Those who withhold income tax shall notify the taxpayer when withholding tax and pay the tax to the local tax collection agency. Those who withhold income tax in the preceding paragraph shall, in addition to declaring interest on bearer securities and interest on deposits with a special form, declare the amount of income of each taxpayer to the local competent tax collection agency.

Article 29: The tax collection agency shall issue a formal receipt prescribed by the competent tax collection agency when it receives the tax withheld in the preceding article.

Article 30: If those who withhold income tax can complete their withholding duties in accordance with the legal procedures and time limit, the local competent tax collection agency may give a bonus of five per thousand of the total amount withheld. The aforementioned bonus shall not apply to government agencies.

Article 31: Those who pay income tax themselves shall pay the income tax to the tax collection agency in accordance with the tax payment period after receiving the notice of the amount of income tax determined by the local competent tax collection agency. Those who pay the above shall obtain a formal receipt prescribed by the competent tax collection agency from the tax collection agency.

Article 32: The competent tax collection agency of the Ministry of Finance shall formulate a notice of the amount of tax payable for each type of income earner and issue it to the local tax collection agencies to notify the taxpayers in accordance with the provisions of Article 14 of the Provisional Regulations.

Article 33: The local competent tax collection agency shall determine the amount of income tax for the declarant within 15 days of receiving the declaration. If the declarant requests a re-investigation, it shall re-determine the amount of tax within 10 days from the date of receiving the request.

Article 34: If the local competent tax collection agency believes that the declarant's declaration is untrue, it may specify a time limit to require the declarant to present documentary evidence related to the amount of tax payable. If the declarant fails to perform the aforementioned request, the local competent tax collection agency may directly determine the amount of income and the amount of tax payable based on investigation or other methods and notify it. When the declarant receives the aforementioned notice, he shall pay the tax within the tax payment period.

Article 35: If the local competent tax collection agency discovers that the amount of tax withheld is insufficient, it shall order the person withholding income tax to pay it in full.

Article 36: If the taxpayer believes that there is an amount of income tax withheld that should be reduced, he may apply to the local competent tax collection agency for a tax refund.

Article 37: The competent tax collection agency of the Ministry of Finance shall formulate declaration forms for each type of income and issue them to the local tax collection agencies for the declarants to collect and fill out themselves. The aforementioned declaration forms may be entrusted by the local tax collection agencies to the local administrative agencies, chambers of commerce, trade associations, post offices, or tax collection agencies to store them for the declarants to collect and announce or post them.

Article 38: No fees may be attached to any declaration form for each type of income.

Article 39: The local competent tax collection agency shall establish a register of each type of income, and record the name, address, occupation income determination, tax payable, and other matters that should be recorded of the taxpayer in accordance with the contents of the declaration form and the determination notice.

Article 40: The income tax amount determination notice shall be numbered and registered according to the type of income.

Article 41: Those who withhold income tax, pay income tax themselves, or pay income tax on behalf of others shall not refuse to present the certificates required by the investigation, review, and audit personnel.

Article 42: If a declarant knowingly declares an untrue amount of income, in addition to being fined or convicted in accordance with Article 19 of the Provisional Regulations, if there is a situation that violates the crime of forging documents in the Criminal Law, the competent tax collection agency shall also report to the court for handling.

Article 43: Personnel of the income tax collection agency shall absolutely keep confidential the income amount, tax amount, and supporting documents of the taxpayer. If they violate this, the supervising officer shall, after verifying the facts, or after the victim reports and the facts are verified, give the supervising officer a dismissal or other disciplinary action. If they violate the Criminal Law, they shall also report to the court for handling.

Article 44: When the local competent tax collection agency imposes a penalty in accordance with the provisions of Articles 18, 19, and 20 of the Provisional Regulations, it shall send a penalty letter to the person being penalized. A receipt shall be given for the penalty paid. The seal of the penalty agency and the name and seal of the responsible person shall be affixed to the aforementioned penalty letter and receipt.

Article 45: When a limited liability company or a limited partnership company issues shares, it shall report the total amount of shares, types of shares, amount per share, and business year to the local competent tax collection agency. For shares that have been issued, the companies shall report the aforementioned matters that should be reported to the local competent tax collection agency within one month from the date of implementation of these Detailed Rules.

Article 46: Companies, commercial firms, shops, factories, and profit-making individuals shall report their name, address, and actual amount of business capital or share capital to the local competent tax collection agency within one month from the date of implementation of these Detailed Rules.

Article 47: The forms, books, and voucher formats specified in these Detailed Rules shall be formulated by the Ministry of Finance.

Article 48: Matters not covered in these Detailed Rules may be amended by the Ministry of Finance at any time with the approval of the Executive Yuan.

Article 49: The date of implementation of these Detailed Rules shall be the date approved by the Executive Yuan. (20th, Central News Agency dispatch)

Japanese Stationed in China; Key Overseas Personnel Gather in Tianjin for Meetings; Four Sessions to Study Various Issues; Important Decisions Still Rest with Senior-Level Meetings

Tianjin Correspondence: Key Japanese army and overseas personnel stationed in China have gathered in Tianjin. Four separate meetings will be held. Aside from the meeting centered around Tashiro and Kawagoe, already held at the Haiguang Temple Barracks at 3 PM on the 17th, meetings hosted by Lieutenant Colonels Kagezo and Nakamura, and Administrative Official Ota, tasked with conveying orders from the three army, navy, and foreign affairs ministries; the North China Consuls meeting hosted by Kawagoe; and the meeting of Special Agency Chiefs hosted by the newly appointed Chief of Staff of the North China Garrison, Hashimoto Gun, have all been postponed by several days due to the late arrival of participants. Chief of Staff Hashimoto arrived in Tianjin via the Northeast on the 18th and assumed his post that same day. Shinkyo Company President, Senkawa Shinji, and Mantetsu’s Tianjin Director, Tanimoto, arrived in Tianjin by train early on the 19th. Ambassador Kawagoe, who had visited Song Zheyuan in Peiping, was permitted to return to Tianjin at 7 PM on the 20th. Army Ministry Military Affairs Bureau Staff Kagezo, Navy Ministry Military Affairs Bureau Staff Nakamura, and Foreign Ministry Administrative Official Ota are scheduled to arrive by plane on the morning of the 20th. Furthermore, the usual Japanese garrison commander Kawabe, military attachés Matsumuro, Hamada, Imai, Tongzhou military attaché Tsunaki, Ueno, Zhangjiakou military attaché Omoto, Suiyuan military attaché Hayama, Jinan military attaché Ishino, and Shanhaiguan military attaché Kuwabara, are also scheduled to arrive in Tianjin on the morning of the 20th or 21st. Jinan Consul General Arino (will be represented by Consul Takahashi), Qingdao Consul General Nishi, Peiping Embassy Secretary Muto, Zhangjiakou Consul Nakané, and Shanhaiguan Consul Fujii will arrive on the 20th and 21st successively. While there were agendas at the Haiguang Temple meeting on the 17th, due to the emphasis on discussions, there were no concrete resolutions, only exchanges of opinions on the planned North China situation and economic cooperation issues. Important consultations are pending the aforementioned three types of meetings. The meeting convened by Kagezo, Nakamura, and Ota is scheduled to be held at 2 PM on the afternoon of the 21st at the Japanese Concession Zhang Garden Commander’s Residence, where the three representatives will declare the three ministries' unified foreign policy approach and relay the views obtained through liaison with the Kwantung Army. The scope of discussions has been slightly altered from the original plan. In addition to reports on matters pertaining to their respective duties from staff members of the stationed army, military attachés, embassy officials, and naval attachés in Peiping and Tianjin, Kubota and Kuwabara, the topics to be discussed include: 1. North China economic development; 2. Sino-Japanese economic cooperation; 3. North China regime; 4. Special trade; 5. Tariff reductions; 6. Chahar-Suiyuan Incident. Tashiro, Kawagoe, Kubota, Hashimoto, and North China army and navy attachés will all attend, with an emphasis on reporting and research. The North China Consuls meeting, originally scheduled for the 20th, has been changed to the 22nd due to Kawagoe's visit to Song Zheyuan in Peiping. The venue will be the Tianjin Consulate General. Foreign Minister Arita sent a telegram to Tianjin on the 19th, instructing on the issues to be studied at this meeting. Therefore, in addition to the aforementioned issues, the following will be added: 1. Adaptation to the North China situation and decision on policy towards China; 2. Concrete policies for North China economic cooperation; 3. Expansion of the Tianjin Consulate General's organization; 4. Strengthening the organization of the North China police authority with the Tianjin Police Department as its core. All discussions will be based on the scope set by the Kagezo, Ota, and Nakamura meeting on the 21st. After the meeting, on the 24th or 25th, Tashiro, Kawagoe, Kubota, Hashimoto, and others will convene the so-called senior-level meeting of relevant organizations stationed in North China, as well as a Special Agency Chiefs meeting. This meeting will focus on creating concrete strategies, summarizing the economic opinions provided by the Shinkyo Company, Mantetsu, and other parties, deciding on the direction of advancement, and handing it over to the three representatives, Kagezo, etc., to take back and report to the central leadership. Kawagoe will then leave Tianjin on the 26th to fly to Jinan to visit Han Fuju and exchange views before flying back to Shanghai. He plans to convene a South and Central China Consuls meeting in Shanghai on the 27th, 28th, and 29th, with the results of the North China discussions as the core agenda, and discuss them once again with the South and Central China consuls. Those confirmed to attend the meeting include Shanghai Consul General Wakasugi, Nanjing Consul General Suma, Hankou Consul General Miura, Guangzhou Consul General Nakamura, and Hong Kong Consul General Mizusawa. (August 19th)

Guizhou Aircraft Defects to Central Government; Zheng Zixiang and Lin Weicheng Leave Guizhou; Four Communications Aircraft Arrive in Guangzhou One After Another

Guangzhou Correspondence: There is still little hope for a peaceful resolution to the Guizhou situation. Guizhou's air force generals, fearing the devastation of the region and internal strife, have long been planning to defect from the Guizhou government. Lin Weicheng (a Guangdong native), the commander of the Guizhou Air Force and principal of the aviation school, has repeatedly planned to lead his squadron out of Guizhou, but since the Guangdong squadron defected to the central government, the Guizhou authorities have been strictly guarding against Guizhou air force personnel, and have placed the deputy principal of the Guizhou Aviation School, Zhong Ji, in charge of all aircraft, prohibiting unauthorized piloting. Even when special missions require flying, fuel is restricted to prevent long-distance travel. Lin Weicheng and others have had no opportunity. They once proposed moving the Guizhou squadron to Guixian under the pretext of defending the border, hoping to fly to Guangdong, but recently the airfields in Guixian and Wuzhou have been flooded, making it impossible to fly. The Guizhou authorities have tightened security over military aircraft. Zheng Zixiang, the captain of the third squadron of the Guizhou Air Force, could no longer wait and, taking advantage of an order to scout the border, led his deputy Li Yifei, squad leader Liang Weiru, and pilot Luo Shumin on the afternoon of the 14th, flying three Guizhou communications aircraft, 703, 705, and 706, departing from Liuzhou, detouring near Yaoshan, and turning into the West River. Midway, due to fuel exhaustion, 703 and 705 were forced to land at the Kaiping County airfield in Guangdong. Only aircraft 706, piloted by Zheng, flew to Guangzhou at 7 PM that evening. Chen Qingyun, the commander of the Central Air Force, greeted them at Tianhe Airfield and introduced them to military authorities the next day. They received encouraging words from Chairman Chiang. Zheng and others then issued a public telegram on the 15th announcing their defection from Guizhou to the central government. After this incident, the Guizhou authorities paid closer attention to the movements of Guizhou air force personnel. Lin Weicheng became increasingly uneasy. On the morning of the 15th, he went to Nanning to report on military affairs, accompanied by Ning Mingjie, the captain of the second squadron of the Guizhou Air Force. As they prepared to depart from Liuzhou on a communications aircraft, Guizhou pilots surrounded Lin, saying that two people did not need to go together to report on military affairs. Lin insisted on going, and they were allowed to depart, but the Guizhou people were still uneasy and sent three aircraft to follow behind, until near Nanning, when they turned back. After arriving in Nanning, Lin met with Li Bai and reported on the air force incident (referring to Zheng Zixiang's escape with three aircraft to Guangdong). For precautionary measures, Li Bai agreed to organize an aviation committee in Nanning, tasked with planning air force combat strategies, but in reality, it was to restrain the pilots. They also planned to transfer Guangdong pilots in Liuzhou to be members. Lin agreed. On the 16th, they requested permission to return to Liuzhou to handle everything. At noon that day, they departed from Nanning. Lin and Ning believed the time had come. After taking off, they turned east and arrived at Tianhe Airfield in Guangzhou at 3 PM, where they met with Chen Qingyun and others and reported on their defection to the central government. It is said that the actual strength of the Guizhou Air Force was initially only 30 aircraft, and recently 40 more were purchased, with a total of over 100 pilots. The Air Force headquarters and airfield hangars are all in Liuzhou, with Guilin, Wuzhou, and Nanning as important stations. In addition to reconnaissance aircraft, there are over 20 fighter aircraft and over 10 bomber aircraft. Li Bai has spared no effort in expanding the air force and has arranged for strict air defense. After Lin and others defected to the central government, they issued a telegram on the 17th declaring their loyalty to the central government, expressing their attitude. On the 18th, Lin Weicheng, Ning Mingjie, Zheng Zixiang, Li Yifei, Liang Weiru, and Luo Shumin jointly issued three documents: one was a letter of advice to Li Bai, one was a letter to the Guizhou military, and one was a letter to the Guizhou Air Force comrades, advising all Guizhou military personnel to change their ways and support the central government. (August 19th)

Tragic State of Flood Disasters in Various Parts of Guangdong Province; Dongjiang Jiaoling Embankment Breached Over 1,000 Zhang; Five Base Embankments Collapsed Along the West River; Six Breaches in Various Embankments in Nanhai

Guangzhou Correspondence: Due to continuous rainfall for the past month, flash floods, and swollen rivers in various parts of Guangdong Province, river embankments have collapsed one after another, causing floods and affecting hundreds of thousands of people. The situation is tragic. Earlier, the Han River in the Chaozhou area, Chenghai County, breached its embankment by over 100 zhang, followed by the collapse of the Chiding and Changli embankments in Zhaoqing on the West River. In recent days, the Guangxi area has experienced wind and rain for ten consecutive days, with floods in the Fu River and major river basins. Wuzhou water levels rose by several zhang, and the lower reaches of the West River continued to rise. The Fengning embankment in Zhaoqing, Guangdong Province, also collapsed. On the 12th, the Xiangshan and Etang embankments in the sixth district of Gaoyao County also collapsed. In Gaoyao County alone, six embankments have collapsed one after another. All the villages within the embankments have become flooded, and late rice and crops have been completely washed away. Victims, young and old, are exposed to the wind and rain, waiting for food. People in the county have purchased rice, salt, and vegetables to distribute to the disaster areas, but this is only a drop in the bucket and cannot provide universal relief. Telegrams have been sent to various parties requesting prompt allocation of funds for relief. As for Jiaoling County in the upper reaches of the Dong River, since the flash flood on June 7, no embankment has remained intact. There are no less than 19 breaches, large and small, on both the east and west banks, inundating countless houses. On the 3rd of this month, the river rose again, and the newly built embankment was broken again, with 16 breaches. The LanShe, SiXi, Shanzhaoshuxia, and Baiqiaoli embankments in the county have a total breach of over 1,000 zhang, with a water depth of over 10 zhang, inundating over 10,000 shi of rice and several thousand houses. The cry for help can be heard everywhere. Unfortunately for the people of Guangdong, they suffered a hurricane on the 16th of the month, with both wind and rain, and the water level of each river increased further. The loss of rice and crops in various parts of the province is incalculable. Along the West River, the embankments along the river are once again showing signs of danger. It was found that the Jingfu embankment in Zhaoqing once breached on the 17th during a violent storm, but fortunately, the villagers blocked it overnight. After a day and night of effort, the situation was turned around. The Zaogang embankment in Sanshui County, located in the key area of the West River, suddenly had its foundations collapse, but fortunately, officials and people came to the rescue, preventing it from collapsing. As for the embankments in Nanhai in the lower reaches, those that collapsed after the 16th include the Bi'an embankment, with a breach of over 9 zhang, and the Dongcun, Shali, Banggang, and Yinkeng embankments, which collapsed one after another. The Jiangwei base embankment had a breach of 7 zhang, the Bangjiang embankment had a breach of over 6 zhang, and the Yinkeng embankment had a breach of over 4 zhang. Disaster victims have been displaced, and the six embankment managers have urgently telegraphed the government for relief. As for the Die embankment in the fourth district of Nanhai, the breach that occurred on the 17th has been repaired, but the villagers are still guarding it day and night, unable to sleep or eat peacefully. Looking at the embankment breaches in various places in recent days, it is precisely when the new grains are ripening, but now they have been swept away. The future of food for the people of Guangdong Province is worrying. (August 17th)

Singapore; New Regulations Issued Again for Overseas Chinese Entering the Country; Nothing More Than Limiting the Increase in the Number of Unemployed

Shantou Correspondence: Chaozhou and Meizhou have suffered from natural and man-made disasters in recent years. The people cannot make a living locally. The young and strong leave their hometowns to seek a way out, and the old and weak often die in ditches. Therefore, since this year, the number of people from various counties in Chaozhou and Meizhou who have gone abroad via Shantou has been increasing daily. In July, more than 8,000 people went abroad via Shantou. However, the number of passenger tickets for ships to Singapore and Malaya is restricted by the local government. Old customers who have lived in Singapore and have residence permits are not restricted by the number of passenger tickets because they have fixed jobs. Each person can buy a first-class ticket for 55 yuan. If there is no residence permit, it is difficult to buy one even for 120 yuan after waiting for the allocation of passenger tickets in the hotel. Because the Singapore government only allows 5,000 passengers to enter the country each month, and Shantou only gets 1,000 passenger tickets according to the quota distributed to the four ports of Hong Kong, Haikou, You Tou, and Xiamen. Due to strict restrictions, cases of using sailboats to smuggle, sneaking into the cabin, or forging residence permits to impersonate old passengers have been found repeatedly in Shantou this year. These unfortunate events are rooted in the world's economic downturn, the instability of Chinese society, and the inability of people to maintain their livelihoods. Now, the Singapore government has issued new regulations for overseas Chinese entering the country, which will be implemented from September 1. The measures are as follows: (1) Overseas Chinese entering the country must have a formal passport from their country. If they want to land in Singapore or travel for two weeks, they must submit two photos of themselves and pay a temporary landing tax of 5 Singapore dollars to the local Immigration Bureau to obtain a landing permit. If they are tourists passing through Singapore or temporarily residing, they can claim back the 5-dollar landing fee from the Immigration Department on the day they leave Singapore. (2) Chinese people who come to Singapore in first or second class must have their Chinese passport signed by the British Consulate in Shantou. When they arrive in Singapore, they must submit two photos and a landing tax of 5 Singapore dollars. However, Chinese people who come to Singapore in steerage class and are workers are exempt from passports, but two photos and a landing fee of 5 Singapore dollars should be paid as usual. (3) New overseas Chinese who come to Singapore from other ports must register with the Foreigners Registration Office in the Chinese People's Political Affairs Building within 48 hours. If it is a Sunday, they must register at the Central Police Station. Those who do not register will be in violation of the law and will be sentenced to a fine of 1,000 Singapore dollars or imprisonment for six months. (4) Chinese people who return to their motherland or return to the south in the near future must obtain a passport from the Chinese Consulate General before leaving Singapore, and at the same time request a visa for the passport from the Foreigners Registration Office. The fee is 6 Singapore dollars. They can also apply for a lower decision entry permit to avoid paying a 5-dollar landing fee when they come to the south in the future. Those who travel to and from steerage class do not need a passport or visa procedures, but must have an entry permit.

Anhui Province Long-Distance Telephone; Telephone Lines with Jiangsu, Henan, Jiangxi, and Hubei Are Open; Branch Lines Are Being Expanded

Bengbu Correspondence: Anhui Province's long-distance telephone service has been actively constructed and promoted by the Ministry of Communications in recent years, and its business development has been quite rapid. In northern Anhui, Bengbu is the central point, and the telegraph office here is responsible for the overall management. The trunk lines are all open, and the branch lines are still being expanded. The copper lines of the nine-province long-distance telephone are being gradually connected, and the calls are very clear. However, the branch lines are iron lines that combine telegrams and telephone, and the sound waves are slightly inferior. The current flows quickly on copper lines, and the iron lines are slower to conduct electricity. Anhui's long-distance telephone trunk and branch lines are connected to neighboring provinces, such as Anhui-Jiangsu, Anhui-Henan, Anhui-Jiangxi, and Anhui-Hubei, and have been opened gradually. According to the investigation, the places that can be called from Bengbu include Huaiyuan, Fengyang, Luohe, Fengtai, Shuangjianji, Longkangji, Shungengshan, Sixian, Wuhe, Mengcheng, Shou County, Zhengyang, Xiyangji, Guoyang, and Huoqiu in northern Anhui; Wuhu, Dangtu, Anqing, Yinjiahui, and Tunxi in southern Anhui; Linhuai, Mingguang, Chuxian, Wuyi, Fuliji, and Su County in the southern section of Jinpu Road; Tongshan, Nanjing, Wujin, Zhenjiang, Yixing, Wuxi, Wu County, Changshu, and Shanghai in Jiangsu Province; Gushi, Kaifeng, and Zhengzhou in Henan Province; Jiujiang, Guling, and Nanchang in Jiangxi Province; and Hankou, Hanyang, and Wuchang in Hubei Province. The calls have only recently started to be opened, but calls from Bengbu must pass through Gujiahui and use a booster to reach Wuhan. It is rumored that the Bengbu Telephone Bureau is also planning to open calls to major stations along the Huainan Railway, and is negotiating the connection method. Once the contract is finalized, it can be realized. In terms of business, it is divided into ordinary calls, express calls, call notification, and advance notification. The fees vary. The business is particularly prosperous during the active grain market season. Currently, the average daily calls are around 200, and the monthly income is over 1,000 yuan. The Bengbu Bureau has one technical person in charge, one engineer, and nine drivers. In terms of treatment, the salary is increased annually according to the assessment. However, the telephone is still a magneto type, divided into wall-mounted and desk-mounted, which is not the latest type of telephone and still needs to be improved to increase efficiency. Long-distance telephones can now be temporarily connected with local telephones, which is very convenient for general users.

Kunshan; Preparing to Build Zhenchuan Park

The An Ting Zhenchuan Academy in the third district of this county was the place where the former sage, Mr. Gui Zhenchuan, taught. The house is spacious, but it has been abandoned due to years of disrepair. The county government, in order to commemorate the former sage, immediately consulted with the authorities of Jiading and Qingpu counties to discuss the plan to transform it into Zhenchuan Park, to provide a place for the public to enjoy. The required reconstruction expenses will be jointly borne by the three counties.

Local Tobacco Store Owner Arrested for Cheating

The Hexing Local Tobacco Paste Store in Qian Dun Town, the fourth district of the county, has continuously sold local tobacco to unlicensed private smokers from May last year to August this year. The number is quite large, totaling more than 500 taels. In the first ten days of this month, the store submitted a request to the county to purchase more tobacco. The county government suspected that the reported inventory was still large, so it immediately sent someone to investigate. It was found that there was a deficit due to private sales, and the store owner Wu Xiong was immediately arrested for investigation.

Wuxi; Robbery Criminal Executed by Firing Squad

On the evening of June 6th of this year, at about 9:00 PM, the Yuanju silk cocoon trading firm in Fangqian Town, the second district of the county, was robbed of 6,532 yuan in cash by several bandits. Later, the Changshu Public Security Fourth Sub-bureau arrested the main criminal, He Yongding (aka He Yongchao), in Gang Kou Town, the fourth district of the county, and seized 1,103 yuan of the original stolen legal tender from the Si Ming Bank. The Muyi Public Security Bureau sent personnel to Yu to welcome and escort them to Wuxi, and transferred them to the court and then to the Second District Security Command for detention. It was then learned that He was a messenger of the 22nd Regiment of the 36th Division. On June 6th, he and another messenger, Long Tao, took the opportunity to escape and rob the Yuanju silk cocoon trading firm. After obtaining the loot, He married a prostitute named Cao Jinnu in Yu, which led to his arrest and escort to Wuxi. Last month, the 26th Division headquarters sent personnel to the Security Command to welcome and escort He, and also arrested the bandit Long Tao in Nanjing and escorted him to Wuxi. After a thorough interrogation by the Military Law Office, it was determined that he had violated Articles 94, Paragraph 3, and 84 of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Criminal Law, and was presented to the Ministry of Military Affairs for approval, and both were sentenced to death. Yesterday (the 20th) at 12:00 noon, the two criminals were brought out, their identities were confirmed, and they were tied up and taken to the Xishan file execution field for execution by firing squad to serve as a warning.

Ancient Tree Blooms with Auspicious Flowers

Near Huizhang Mountain in Nanfangquan, the third district, there is a temple called Dadidian that houses a statue of Zhang Dadi. The temple is spacious, and in the courtyard in front of the temple, there are two ancient yingchunhua trees (also known as Yulan flowers) that are hundreds of years old. For decades, they have never bloomed, and look like dead trees. This year, they were still withered, but at the beginning of this month, the trees suddenly bloomed with auspicious flowers, the yellow ones like gold, the white ones like silver, and the green ones like jade, with colorful colors and a fragrant scent. Nearby residents came to watch in an endless stream, and all praised it as a miracle.

Smuggled Opium Found in Postal Package

The county's postal administration recently received a postal package from Shaoyang, Hunan, addressed to Gu Yuantai Leather Goods Store, No. 62 Nancang Dou, Wuxi. It was wrapped in oiled paper and looked suspicious. Before the package was sent to Wuxi, an unknown person inquired at the bureau. After the package was sent to Wuxi, no one claimed it. The bureau director Shen Fengzheng ordered a postman to investigate Nancangmen, but there was no Gu Yuantai Leather Goods Store there. He reported to the inspector Gu of the Wuxi Customs Office, and together with section member Wang Dunyin of the county government, they went to the post office yesterday morning at 10:00 AM to meet with Director Shen and Li Wenbo and others to open the package for inspection. Inside were five leather tubes and six bags of opium. After weighing it, it weighed 3,150 grams. It was taken to the county and reported to Magistrate Long for review.

The Wuyi County Chamber of Commerce held an emergency meeting of various industries on the morning of the 19th, chaired by Jiang Weixian. The Wuxi-Chengjiang Long-Distance Bus Company has recently spent a lot of money repairing bridges. Hangzhou; New Public Debt Exchange Method

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance issued 60 million in reorganization public debt, and entrusted the Shanghai Commercial Press to print it. The first batch is scheduled to be delivered on August 28, stamped, and new tickets will be exchanged from September 5. The method of exchanging old coupons has been passed by the provincial government, and the Hangzhou Central, China, Communications, and Zhejiang Local Banks have been entrusted to handle it. The public debt exchanged should be allocated to Daxing first. If the ticket holder needs small tickets, he should pay a printing fee of 1.25 per thousand according to the face value. If there are no China, Communications, or local bank branches or offices in the counties outside the province, they can be sent to the county government for exchange, and the county government will issue temporary receipts, which will be transferred to the provincial bank for exchange of new tickets and issued to the ticket holders in accordance with the prescribed procedures.

Borrow 400,000 for Warehouse Construction

The Zhejiang Construction Department is preparing to build five major agricultural warehouses, and has specially appointed commissioners to investigate the construction and equipment of agricultural warehouses in Jiangsu and Anhui provinces. They have returned to the province and are drafting a report to be submitted to the department for reference. The Zhejiang Agricultural Warehouse Management Committee is scheduled to hold its establishment meeting on the 25th. The directors of the major warehouses will be appointed to start preparations for construction, which can be realized in mid-September. The construction cost is 400,000 yuan, which will be borrowed from the Agricultural Bank of China. The draft contract has also been drafted, using 200,000 yuan of reorganized public debt and the major warehouse as collateral. The revolving fund will be lent by the bank up to 3 million without limitation. It can be signed after both parties agree to the amendments.

Nantong; Suppressing and Arresting Mutinous Soldiers

The mutinous soldiers of Sijiao killed Captain Shen and District Chief Ling, and then went to sea by boat. They are now wandering on the ocean as bandits, harassing various fields. Zhu Aizhou, the third district chief of the Provincial Maritime Public Security Bureau stationed in Tong, has sent a team to go to sea from Lvsi to suppress and arrest the mutinous soldiers.

Steps to Improve Cotton Production

The Jiangsu Provincial Cotton Production Improvement Office was established in Nantong. It first started to prevent and control diseases and insect pests, and conduct cultivation experiments and breed fine varieties in Tong and Yancheng, the two major cotton-producing areas in northern Jiangsu. This autumn, the flower banks will be implemented for unified management. A cotton industry improvement fee of 20 cents will be collected for each load of cotton, which is expected to collect 260,000 yuan. In addition to the necessary uses for research and experimentation, all the funds will be stored as a deposit for buying improved cotton seeds.

Cixi, Great Fire in Wayaocun, Cibei

The residents of Wayaocun, Minghechang, Cibei, all make a living by firing kilns. The fuel for the kilns is piled up near the kilns, totaling hundreds of stacks. On the evening of the 16th, at around 9 o'clock, Xu Ashui, a kiln owner, used a winnowing fan to shovel out furnace ash. The embers in the ash were not extinguished. Due to the strong wind, the embers scattered and flew, immediately igniting the pine needles piled up, which could not be contained. This resulted in a major disaster. Firefighters from nearby rushed to put out the fire. Due to the strong wind, the fire was not extinguished until after 3 o'clock. A total of twenty to thirty small houses, six coffins, and dozens of bundles of pine needles were burned down, with estimated losses of no less than two thousand taels of silver.

Ningbo, Corruption of Field Tax Collectors

Chen Qiusui, a field tax collector in Yin County, did not report the grain arrears of landowners to the county for collection. Instead, he arbitrarily charged interest and exploited the public for his own benefit. After being reported by a landowner, the Yin County government arrested him and seized his property as collateral, sealing up his houses and furniture in Jiangshan. The arrears have already been partially paid by the tax collector, who handed in five hundred yuan in cash. He also provided a shop guarantor for six hundred and nine yuan and was temporarily released on bail. However, his family filed a complaint with the court, accusing him of abuse of power and illegal detention. The court sent an official letter to the county government to investigate and report back. It is reported that the Zhejiang Provincial Finance Department's Field Tax Supervision Committee, together with the Yin County government, jointly sent an official letter to the Yin County Local Court Procuratorate, attaching the seized account books that recorded the collection of compound interest at a rate of two percent per month from landowners, requesting that it be investigated and dealt with according to the law.

Cotton Industry Statistics Association Announced Yesterday, This Year's National Cotton Production Estimate, Cotton Field Area Over 300 Million Mu, Output Increased About Double Compared to Last Year

The China Cotton Industry Statistics Association released its first estimate report on national cotton production this year at 5:00 PM yesterday. The cotton fields in the twelve major cotton-producing provinces totaled more than 50 million mu, producing more than 16 million dan of ginned cotton, the highest number in the past 20 years, which can be described as a bumper harvest. Compared with last year, the increase in cotton fields and output reached more than double, because all provinces actively promoted cotton planting and the weather was suitable at the time of sowing, so the area of cotton fields increased. The rainfall has been favorable from the time of sowing to the present, and the growth is very good, so cotton production has greatly increased. The new cotton will be on the market successively within two weeks, and the factories are preparing to start work. The details are listed below:

Increase in Cotton Fields, Bumper Cotton Harvest

The area of cotton fields in each province is: Hebei Province 9,497,177 mu, an increase of 3,181,207 mu compared to last year; Shandong Province 6,091,514 mu, an increase of 4,290,372 mu; Shanxi Province 2,095,932 mu, an increase of 1,028,030 mu; Henan Province 6,056,634 mu, an increase of 4,261,274 mu; Shaanxi Province 4,235,191 mu, an increase of 578,177 mu; Hubei Province 8,458,705 mu, an increase of 3,890,366 mu; Hunan Province 744,720 mu, an increase of 373,532 mu; Jiangxi Province 235,530 mu, an increase of 35,790 mu; Anhui Province 1,420,000 mu, an increase of 89,547 mu; Jiangsu Province 10,493,486 mu, an increase of 235,933 mu; Zhejiang Province 1,722,087 mu, a decrease of 37,405 mu; Sichuan Province 1,263,080 mu, an increase of 2,088,344 mu, totaling 55,041,066 mu, an increase of 20,015,172 mu compared to last year. The output of ginned cotton is: Hebei Province 2,975,297 dan, an increase of 808,850 dan; Shandong Province 1,848,849 dan, an increase of 1,441,634 dan; Shanxi Province 625,528 dan, an increase of 372,936 dan; Henan Province 1,496,276 dan, an increase of 1,079,498 dan; Shaanxi Province 1,147,775, an increase of 345,722 dan; Hubei Province 3,022,394 dan, an increase of 2,105,210 dan; Hunan Province 294,390 dan, an increase of 152,196 dan; Jiangxi Province 59,705 dan, an increase of 17,224 dan; Anhui Province 545,300 dan, an increase of 337,221 dan; Jiangsu Province 2,434,543 dan, an increase of 456,923 dan; Zhejiang Province 666,057 dan, an increase of 204,121 dan; Sichuan Province 1,263,080 dan, an increase of 814,748 dan, totaling 16,379,194 dan. The average yield per mu is 30 jin, the highest number in the past 20 years.

Domestic Cotton Consumption is Approximately 10 Million Dan

The new cotton will be on the market successively within two weeks. Although there are a small number of transactions in various places, they are for local yarn factories to purchase for their own use. In two weeks, it will be shipped to Shanghai in batches. As for the market price of cotton, the current price is higher because the inventory of old cotton is not large. After the new cotton is on the market, it will drop slightly, but the difference will not be too large and will not last long. This year's cotton harvest is a good one, and when the new cotton comes on the market, the price will not change too much in one or two months because the yarn factories will compete to purchase it, and the new cotton will be shipped in batches. It is estimated that the national cotton consumption is around 10 million dan. After each factory has purchased enough goods, the remaining cotton will be forced to drop in price due to sluggish sales. The only way out for this surplus cotton is to be exported to Japan. The country used to obtain raw materials for spinning around 20 counts of coarse yarn from India. If China's cotton price is low, it will definitely take the opportunity to purchase from China. In the Sino-Japanese economic cooperation advocated by the Japanese side, the supply of cotton raw materials is also an important item. It is reported that they are currently negotiating investment in North China and have decided to plant cotton. After this becomes a reality next year, they will use economic power to buy up Chinese cotton at low prices.

Closed Yarn Factories Prepare to Start Work

According to reporters' inquiries to the financial sector, there are approximately 2.8 million spindles in yarn factories across the country, of which 700,000 spindles, including those of Japanese and British merchants, are currently shut down. This year, (1) the cotton harvest is good, and the purchase price of raw materials is expected to be slightly reduced; (2) the selling price of yarn and cloth is also high, and the inventory is relatively small; (3) all agricultural products have bumper harvests, and people's purchasing power is expected to increase; (4) since the suppression of the Guangdong incident, the situation has become more stable. Therefore, yarn merchants are preparing to start their machines one after another. Among them, 300,000 spindles that have been shut down have decided to start work, 300,000 spindles are running around negotiating, and the remaining 100,000 spindles cannot start work due to outdated equipment. The financial sector's investment in various factories has accumulated to 100 million yuan over the years. It is estimated that the operating funds required for the 600,000 spindles of yarn machines that are preparing to resume operations this year is 600,000 yuan per 10,000 spindles, which requires 16 million yuan. If the manufacturers have 20-30% of their own funds, the financial sector is also willing to help them start work. According to the current market price of yarn and cotton, if the operation is prudent, each piece of yarn can make a profit of five or six yuan.

National Election Office Approves Newspaper Reporters Association to Participate in the Election, and Replied According to Article 18 of the Election Law, the Nomination of Candidates is Not Limited to Members of the Association in Each Place

According to the Central News Agency, the City Newspaper Reporters Association has been established for more than four years, but the registration procedures have not yet been completed. In order to maintain the spirit of democracy, it specially petitioned the National Assembly Shanghai City Representative Election Office to be allowed to participate in the election, and sent a letter requesting an explanation of whether the nomination of candidates for freelance professional representatives to the National Assembly is limited to members of the association in each place. The National Assembly Shanghai City Representative Election Office instructed and approved the association to participate in the election, and replied that according to Article 18 of the Representative Election Law, the nomination of candidates is not limited to members of the association in each place. The reporter specially asked the relevant parties to transcribe the original petition of the association and the approval of the Election Office as follows:

Petition for Participation

The original text of the association's petition for approval to participate in the election states: Respectfully, this association was established in accordance with the legal procedures of the Republic of China in 1932. On June 24 of that year, a founding conference was held. Chen Kecheng from the Municipal Government and Chen Lengseng from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau were sent to guide the meeting. Fifteen first-term executive committee members, including Ma Chonggan, seven alternate executive committee members, including Qian Hua, nine supervisory committee members, including Yan Duhe, and five alternate supervisory committee members, including Tang Huiping, were elected that day. The executive and supervisory committee members took office on July 1. Zhu Yangwu from the City Party Headquarters and Chen Kecheng from the Municipal Government supervised the oath-taking. Subsequently, at the general meetings of members and the inauguration of executive and supervisory committee members, the Party and government agencies sent personnel to guide and supervise the oath-taking. The City Party Headquarters issued Permit No. 137 and a certificate proving the soundness of the organization on March 17, 1933. This association applied to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for registration and certification in April 1933, and attached a certificate from the City Party Headquarters proving the soundness of the organization. However, the procedure for filling out the registration form has not been completed, and the registration has not been formally completed. This is the process of the organization and establishment of this association. For the election of representatives to the National Assembly, this association has complied with the order to prepare and report various registers, and the members have taken the civil oath on the 17th of this month. Representative Huang Xianggu, sent by your office, presided over the oath-taking. The organization and establishment of this association has been over four years, the organization is sound, and it has been recognized by the local high-level Party Headquarters. It seems that it is factually in accordance with the provisions of Article 19 of the National Assembly Representative Election Law that it is legally established, but the registration procedures are slightly incomplete. Therefore, we specially state the facts and request that you examine and approve our participation in the election. Respectfully submitted to the National Assembly Shanghai City Representative Election Office, Shanghai Newspaper Reporters Association, August 19, 1936.

Request for Explanation

The original letter from the association requesting an explanation of why the nomination of candidates should not be limited to members of the association in each place states: Respectfully, regarding the method of nominating candidates for freelance professional representatives to the National Assembly, according to the Election Law and the Detailed Rules for Implementation, it seems that when staff from newspaper reporters associations in various places nominate candidates, the candidates are not limited to members of the association in each place. For example, staff from the Shanghai Newspaper Reporters Association can also nominate members of newspaper reporters associations in other places as candidates. However, according to a report on the 16th of this month, a Central News Agency dispatch from Nanjing on the 15th, the election process of the Freelance Professional Group Representative Election Office, "(1) Notify freelance professional groups in all provinces and cities to quickly prepare registers and send them to the local registration authority for review and announcement, and forward them to the office before August 20; (2) Each freelance professional group should immediately nominate candidates based on the announced roster and forward the results of the ballot opening to this office by the fastest method before August 31," whether the candidates are not limited to members of the association in each place is not clearly stipulated. Some members of this association have questions about this. Therefore, we respectfully request that your office provide an explanation to facilitate the process. Respectfully submitted to the National Assembly Shanghai City Representative Election Office, Shanghai Newspaper Reporters Association, August 19, 1936.

Approval to Participate

Instruction No. 9 of the National Assembly Shanghai City Representative Election Office states: A letter has been received, stating that the association has been established for more than four years, the organization is sound, but the registration procedures have not yet been completed, and requesting approval to participate in the election. It is hereby acknowledged that regarding professional elections, this office has now received Instruction No. 42 of the National Assembly Representative Election General Office, which states, "Organizations that have been guided and permitted by the Party Headquarters and are still applying for registration can be regarded as legal organizations." The association's request to be allowed to participate in the election should be approved, and you should comply accordingly. This order, August 20, 1936, Supervisor Wu Tiecheng.

Explanation of Doubts

The original letter from the National Assembly Shanghai City Representative Election Office replying to the inquiry on whether the nomination of candidates is not limited to members of the association in each place states: In reply, we have received your letter regarding whether the nomination of candidates for freelance professional representatives to the National Assembly is not limited to members of the association in each place, and members of this association have questions about this, requesting an explanation to be sent to the office. The Election Law for Representatives to the National Assembly, Article 18, already stipulates that the nomination of candidates by freelance professional groups is not limited to members of the association in each place. This reply is for your information. Respectfully to the Shanghai Newspaper Reporters Association, National Assembly Shanghai City Representative Election Office, August 20.

The China General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government yesterday, saying, "Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government, greetings. Foreign Banks Settle and Remit, Entrust Bank of China to Act as Agent, Citibank First to Implement, HSBC and Other Banks Will Follow

According to Xin Xin News Agency, foreign banks in this city have always employed staff from Chinese managers (i.e., trade offices) to handle settlement and remittance for Chinese merchants, banks, and money shops. It is reported that Citibank, a US-owned bank, considering the many inconveniences in practice, started last month to entrust the Bank of China to act as its agent for settlement and remittance. The Bank of China gives interest of 1 li on all deposited funds. Since its implementation, both parties have found it convenient. It is also reported that foreign banks such as HSBC, Mercantile Bank of India, Australia and China, The British Bank of the Middle East, and Banque Belge pour l'Etranger, in view of the convenience of Citibank entrusting a Chinese bank to act as its agent for settlement and remittance, will follow suit. This is a memorable event in financial history.

According to Hua Dong News Agency, the compradors of various foreign banks learned of this matter and were panicked, all believing that over a thousand office workers would be in danger of losing their jobs. They elected representatives to petition the Bank of China authorities, requesting that the agency for settlement and remittance be canceled. In order to take into account the livelihoods of over a thousand comprador staff from foreign banks, the bank canceled the agency within days, and will discuss it again after a proper solution is found.

Central Mint Takes Over National Mint Bureaus, Investigates Machine and Housing Conditions, Sends Personnel to Draft Reorganization Measures

According to Hua Dong News Agency, in order to unify minting rights, the Ministry of Finance specially ordered the custodians of the old mint bureaus in Hangzhou, Wuchang, Chengdu, Chongqing, Lanzhou, Tianjin, and Beiping to hand over all the mint bureaus to the Central Mint for management, so that they can measure the situation in various places and allocate the powers of the various mint bureaus across the country, unify minting, and complete the new currency policy.

Central Takeover

After receiving the order, the custodians of the mint bureaus in various places have reported on the machines, houses, detailed internal conditions, past achievements, and annual expenses, respectively. The Central Mint has also sent experts to various mint bureaus to investigate. The statistics have now been completed, and the reorganization and application methods can be drafted in the shortest time and reported to the Ministry of Finance for approval.

Future Measures

A reporter from Hua Dong News Agency inquired with relevant parties yesterday morning and learned that the Central Mint will start reorganization after investigation and clarification. In the future, the existing machinery of each mint bureau will be the initial stage of reorganization. If the machinery of Mint A matches that of Mint B, it will be moved for use. According to the financial sector, this type of machinery is also suitable for the minting of new subsidiary coins, and some can even print legal tender.

County Land Administration Bureau Explains Land Value Tax Collection Method, Classifies Land and Estimates Value, No Additional Taxes Besides Land Value Tax

Since Shanghai County is implementing land value tax for the first time this year, it is an unprecedented event. A few days ago, Qin Xitian, the chairman of the County Local Association, sent a letter to the County Land Administration Bureau asking about two points of doubt: (1) Besides the 1% land value tax, will the original surcharge tax still be levied? (2) After the tidal fields in the reed marshes are upgraded to arable land, will they also be assessed at an average land value of 100 yuan per mu, the same as rural land? Director Jin Yanzhe replied with a letter yesterday explaining the truth. The original letter is recorded below: In reply, I have received your letter. The land value tax in this county is collected in two installments at a tax rate of 1% of the assessed land value. All surcharges have been abolished. The average land value of rural land in this county is just over 100 yuan per mu. The land value tax has been reduced by 1 jiao and 5 fen compared to the old field tax. The implementation of the land value tax can average the burden on the people, which is not an exaggeration. It is not true that additional taxes still need to be levied besides the 1% land value tax. This time, the land value of rural land in this county is divided into four types of land value areas: residential land, farmland and miscellaneous land, open ground, state-owned gardens, graveyard wasteland, pond rivers, and reed marshes. The standard land values are: residential land, the highest price is 130 yuan per mu, and the lowest price is 115 yuan; farmland and miscellaneous land, the highest price is 109 yuan, and the lowest price is 96 yuan; graveyard wasteland, the highest price is 74 yuan, and the lowest price is 65 yuan; pond rivers, the highest price is 32 yuan, and the lowest price is 25 yuan. If the land has special circumstances, it will be estimated separately and listed as a special land value, and will be notified separately in accordance with the law. Although the coastal reed marshes have been upgraded to arable land, the tax will be lightened due to the lower land value, and there will be no increase in the burden. The chairman reported at the 15th Land Reorganization Discussion Committee that the estimated land value of rural land is 100 yuan per mu, which refers to the average, and it does not mean that the land value of reed marshes and tidal flats is taxed at 100 yuan per mu. The main purpose of implementing the land value tax is to levy taxes based on value, equalize the burden on the people, eliminate the accumulated malpractices of the field tax, increase government revenue, and promote the development of local undertakings. It is the most reasonable and fair tax system in modern times. The Premier spoke in detail in his testament. Land surveys and land registration in this county have been completed one after another. We have been ordered by the province to promote it first. Under the command of the Premier's land policy, Yanzhe will do his best to actively implement it, so as to see its completion as soon as possible. However, it is an unprecedented event, and we hope that local talents will help, so that it can be promoted without hindrance. I am honored to have been inquired about and truthfully reported the facts. I hope you will take notice.

Guangdong Borrows from Three Banks, Already Disbursed 3 Million Yuan, Two More Installments at the End of August and Mid-September, Rumors of Increased Borrowing are Untrue

The Guangdong Provincial Government, in order to reorganize its finances, borrowed 6 million yuan from the Bank of China, the Central Bank, and the Bank of Communications, with the province's tax revenue as collateral. The contract was signed in Guangdong at the end of July. The Guangdong branches of the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications are directly disbursing the funds. As for the Central Bank, because its Guangzhou branch is still under preparation, it has entrusted the Guangzhou branch of the Bank of China to handle the matter. The contract stipulates that the funds will be disbursed in four installments, each installment being 1.5 million yuan, with two installments per month. Two installments have already been disbursed at the end of July and on August 15th. The rumor that another 4 million yuan has been borrowed is untrue, as the previous loan has not yet been fully disbursed.

Large Quantities of Shandong Zhoucun Serge and Tweed Dumped in Shanghai, Suspected of Being Smuggled Goods, The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Has Inquired with the Local Chamber of Commerce for Details, The National Goods Year Meeting Asks the Anti-Smuggling Association to Prevent It

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the number of Minghua Serge and Zhongshan Tweed from Zhoucun, Shandong, has recently increased sharply in the local silk market, with about five or six thousand bolts being transported to Shanghai every day, endlessly. The Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Year Movement, considering that these rayon fabrics are being dumped at low prices, which greatly hinders the local Chinese weaving factories, has separately sent letters to silk merchants, requesting them to refuse to purchase them, and also requested the anti-smuggling associations to prevent it, in order to maintain the domestic silk industry. The original letters are transcribed as follows: (1) Gentlemen, it has been found that Minghua Serge and Zhongshan Tweed from Zhoucun, Shandong, have recently been dumped at low prices in the market, which is very rampant. As many as five or six thousand bolts are transported to Shanghai by post every day. According to the wholesale price in Shanghai, Zhongshan Tweed costs 3.3 yuan per 2.5 pounds of domestic currency, and Minghua Serge costs 4 yuan per 3 pounds of domestic currency, which is very different from similar products in Shanghai. The raw material cost of Shanghai Tweed per 2.5 pounds already requires 3.6 yuan. As for Shanghai Minghua Serge, not to mention the raw material cost, the tax alone requires 4.2 yuan per 3 pounds of rayon. The huge difference in price is shocking. At a time when tax evasion and smuggling have become a major problem for the people's industry and commerce, the source and cause of this dumping of rayon fabrics are very obvious. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, concerned about the operation of Shanghai factories, has specially sent a letter to the Zhoucun Chamber of Commerce to inquire about the details. This Association deeply feels that if the flow of these dumping goods to Shanghai is not stopped, the Shanghai silk industry will likely collapse, and the outflow of profits will be incalculable. Therefore, this special letter is sent to you, sincerely requesting you to consider the difficulties of the time, refuse to purchase these dumping goods, and maintain the operation of domestic factories. We are very much looking forward to it. (2) Gentlemen, since your Association has led all sectors of society to strictly crack down on smuggling, smuggled goods in this city have gradually decreased. This is indeed a good phenomenon to save industry and commerce and stabilize the market. However, recently, Minghua Serge and Zhongshan Tweed from Zhoucun, Shandong, have increased sharply in Shanghai, reaching as many as five or six thousand bolts per day. Considering the low price, which is unexpected, it is not difficult to judge that it is a disguised form of smuggled goods. Thinking that the difficulties of the time are increasing day by day, and it is difficult for domestic silk factories to maintain, if dumping of smuggled goods is allowed again, the future will be even more unimaginable. In addition to sending letters to various silk merchants to refuse to purchase these dumping goods, we sincerely request your Association to prevent it, in order to maintain the domestic silk industry. We are deeply grateful.

China Construction Bank Corporation Half-Year Business Report

Since the establishment of the China Construction Bank Corporation two years ago, its foundation has become increasingly solid, and its reputation at home and abroad has gradually improved. Its operating performance in the recent six months has been even more remarkable. It is truly a dawn for the future of economic construction in our country. A reporter from the Xinxin News Agency obtained the company's business report for the first half of this year as follows:

Assisting in Promoting Railway Construction

It is one of the important businesses of the company's original policy to assist the government in promoting and constructing important railways across the country. Therefore, at the beginning of its establishment, it immediately started the completion of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, and the construction of the Qiantang River Bridge is the main task to complete the road. Therefore, the company raised the construction funds in order to complete the work. Other examples include the purchase of cars and materials for the Longhai Road, the collection of construction funds for the Chengdu-Chongqing Road, and the payment of steamed wood bridges for the Sujia Road, which are either actively in progress or have already been agreed upon. These are all important undertakings of the company at present.

Supporting Transportation and Public Utilities

In the spring of this year, the Ministry of Transportation, in order to reorganize and develop various transportation undertakings across the country, had discussed with the company and other banks to borrow 5 million yuan of national currency, so that various facilities could be decided and held. In addition, the capital telephone is of great importance to increasing the efficiency of government agencies. Therefore, the company also assisted in the expansion of the capital telephone plan of the Ministry of Transportation. In addition, the Jiangxi Provincial Government previously requested the company to raise funds for the construction of the Nanchang Hydropower Plant. The company negotiated with foreign merchants and established a credit purchase loan of 104,000 pounds sterling. The contract has been signed and construction can start in a short period of time.

Net Profit of One Million in the First Half of the Year

In addition, the company has assisted other companies in their operations and planned various enterprises, some of which are in scale or are being designed. The company also provides assistance to the government in terms of short-term financial needs. All of these are deeply gratifying to the shareholders. The final accounts for the first half of the year show that the profit income is 1,438,531.26 yuan, the operating expenses are 94,038.39 yuan, the real estate management expenses are 12,255.98 yuan, and the interest expenses are 11,986.47 yuan. After offsetting the income and expenses, the net profit is 1,230,250.042 yuan.

Autumn House Tax in the City, The Finance Bureau Sends Staff to Collect, And Abolishes the Self-Payment Method

The Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau announced that since the city's house tax was changed to allow households with quarterly taxes of more than 10 yuan to pay by themselves within a specified period in the 24th year, residents have often been delayed due to events, or it is inconvenient due to the distance, resulting in penalties for exceeding the deadline, which has increased the extra burden. The Bureau is now planning to reorganize the collection of autumn house tax starting from September 1st of this year for the sake of considering the tax households. The self-payment method will be abolished, and staff will be sent to collect the tax on a quarterly basis regardless of the amount of the tax. The tax tickets will be changed to numbered receipts, which will be temporarily filled in by the collectors according to the roster and given to each household to facilitate convenience. In addition to submitting it to the municipal government for approval for trial implementation, it is also announced to the residents in the territory for information.

Liang Shao Wine Stores Resumed Business Yesterday Morning, Workers Stopped Work, Resumed After Persuasion, Negotiating to Guarantee Workers' Work This Morning

After the employees of the Shanghai Liang Shao Wine Trade Association members Tongchangfu and Tongheyong wine stores were released on bail, the association announced the resumption of business yesterday morning. However, the wine delivery workers of various wine stores stopped work, demanding guarantees. They agreed to resume work after persuasion and scheduled to negotiate a guarantee method today. The details are recorded as follows:

Announcement of Resumption of Business

After the detained employees were released on bail, the association immediately notified the member wine stores by telephone to resume business the night before yesterday, and reissued a notice yesterday saying, Gentlemen, because the inspectors of the inspection office indiscriminately seized wines, detaining the store clerks, so that the whole body could not operate freely. Therefore, a temporary membership meeting was held on the 17th of this month, and it was decided to suspend wholesale business. On the one hand, He Xiangsheng and others were elected as representatives to go to the Consolidated Tax Bureau to petition. As a result, the Tongchangfu store clerk and the Tongheyong wine ship were released on bail. The prerequisite problem has been resolved. In addition to continuing to negotiate by the original representatives, it is necessary to restore wholesale business first to avoid intangible losses. This special notice is given to various treasure banks for reference, to resume business and unload as usual. All other follow-up issues are waiting to be resolved. This announcement.

Workers Stop Work

The 42 Liang Shao wine stores, including Tongxinchang, resumed business yesterday morning and resumed wholesale transactions. The orders from previous customers were also delivered as usual. The wine ships from Jiangbei, which had been stopped at the Xinchang Bridge, were also resumed. However, after Tongxinchang resumed business, at 8 o'clock yesterday morning, a wine delivery team was delivering wine to Nanshi. When they reached the junction of Fangbang Road and the Chinese and French Concession, they were seen by the inspectors of the Shanghai Inspection Office who wanted to detain them. The wine delivery workers retreated into the concession and detoured, so they were spared. Therefore, the wine delivery workers of various wine stores, a total of 160 people, believed that there was no guarantee for their work, so they stopped work to demand guarantees.

Collective Discussion on Guarantee

The wine delivery workers of 42 wine stores, including Tongchangfu, believing that the inspectors of the Shanghai Inspection Office of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang and Anhui Consolidated Tax Bureau unreasonably arrested people and regarded wine delivery work as a daunting task, and that the workers delivered wine on the orders of the store owner, if there was an alcohol filling incident, the store owner should be responsible, and the wine delivery workers should not be detained. Therefore, at 9 o'clock yesterday morning, a meeting was held at the wine trade association in Maojia Lane, Nanshi, attended by more than 50 workers, chaired by Wang Afang. After reporting the purpose of the meeting, a resolution was made on the spot, demanding guarantees. Before there was a guarantee method, work would be suspended, and Wang Afang and others were appointed to petition the trade association to make demands and provide guarantees.

Persuading to Resume Work

The trade association, because the workers of various wine stores stopped work, so that the wine purchased by various customers was not delivered, specially summoned the workers' representative Wang Afang and others at 3 pm yesterday. Committee member He Xiangsheng persuaded the workers that the trade association was responsible for negotiating with the Jiangnan, Zhejiang and Anhui Consolidated Tax Bureau on the issue of guaranteeing work. However, it was hoped that the workers would work with peace of mind. The workers of various wine stores accepted the persuasion and resumed wine delivery work at 5 pm.

Negotiating Guarantee

The reporter of Xinsheng News Agency met He Xiangsheng, a member of the trade association, late at night. According to him, various wine stores resumed business uniformly on the morning of the 20th. Regarding the workers' strike and demand for guarantees, they also resumed work that night after persuasion. As for the issue of guaranteeing the work of the Baogong team, it was decided that at 9 am on the 21st, he and Section Chief Jiang of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang and Anhui Consolidated Tax Bureau and Section Chief Xia of the Shanghai Inspection Office would negotiate, because the workers are third parties and should not be punished in place of the store owner. In addition, the association has submitted the whole process to the Consolidated Tax Bureau, requesting that the inspection personnel who forcibly detain people and goods be punished, and attached two bottles of alcohol and local burnt samples.
