French Concession Newly Revised Land Tax Regulations

The French Concession Public Works Bureau has recently revised the land tax regulations, which are transcribed as follows: (General Provisions) Article 1: All property owners or perpetual leaseholders in the French Concession, except for the circumstances stipulated in Articles 6 and 7 of the Agreement of April 8, 1914, shall pay land tax. The tax rate and its standard, Article 2: The amount of tax is calculated in proportion to the total value of the real estate land. This calculation shall be verified by the Board of Directors of this Bureau every year and listed in the tax table. Article 3: When preparing the budget every year, this Bureau stipulates that the real estate of the entire concession or a designated part of the concession should be re-evaluated for the current year. Article 4: The Board of Directors shall also organize a real estate valuation committee to carry out the re-evaluation affairs stipulated in the above article. The committee shall be composed of three members, one of whom shall be a director of this Bureau and is the chairman of the committee. The other two members shall be one person selected from the real estate committee established by Decree No. 19 of the French Consul General in Shanghai on December 16, 1919, and Decree No. 40 of March 15, 1930, and one person selected from the property owners designated by the French Consul General. The list of these landowners shall be announced when approving the budget. The above-mentioned real estate valuation committee is entrusted by this Bureau and performs the duties of an appraiser. Article 5: After the value of each piece of real estate is estimated, the estimated amount shall be notified to the landowner or perpetual leaseholder at any time. The person concerned may, within 21 days after receiving this letter, lodge a protest with this Bureau, which shall be reviewed by the Real Estate Committee convened by this Bureau. If the landowner or the perpetual leaseholder applies to attend the meeting, he may be allowed to speak at the meeting. Within eight days after the Real Estate Committee announces the judgment, it shall notify the Bureau and the landowner or the perpetual leaseholder of the results of its deliberation separately. Article 6: If the taxpayer or this Bureau is dissatisfied with the land price stipulated in the second review, both parties may request arbitration by the Real Estate Committee organized by Decree No. 19 of the French Consul General on December 16, 1919, and Decree No. 4 of March 15, 1930. This application for relief shall be submitted within 21 days after receiving the notice stipulated in the above article. The committee shall handle it according to the procedures and conditions stipulated in the above-mentioned decree. Each party shall also be summoned to attend the hearing. The deliberations of the committee shall be conducted in secret, but its judgment shall be announced. Article 7: If the landowner or the perpetual leaseholder does not protest the valuation of his land within the period stipulated in Article 5, or does not apply for relief during the second review by the Real Estate Valuation Committee within the period stipulated in Article 6, he shall be deemed to have accepted the valuation of the property and shall not raise any objection until the re-evaluation. Anyone who requests arbitration from the Real Estate Committee shall be deemed willing to accept its arbitration and obey its resolution as the final judgment, and shall not raise any objection until the re-evaluation. The same shall apply if this Bureau requests arbitration from the committee. Article 8: After the Real Estate Valuation Committee or the Real Estate Committee makes a judgment, or after the relief procedure period expires, this Bureau shall verify the basis for calculating the land tax, and the decision shall be implemented by the various agencies of this Bureau. The procedure is as follows: (1) Formulation of the real estate valuation of a certain part of the concession; (2) Drawing of the land register map (sub-map). The above-mentioned documents shall remain in effect until the future re-evaluation and re-drawing of the new map. The land register is in the form of a registered name, and the property certificate number, land register number, area, value per acre, and land section are noted. (Clearing) Article 9: The Finance Department of this Bureau shall prepare the land tax book according to the land register, copy a page, and distribute it to the landowners or perpetual leaseholders, stating the amount of land tax payable every six months. All transfers of property rights and other matters that may affect the collection of land tax shall be recorded in the book by this Bureau after it becomes aware of them. Collection of tax Article 10: The method of collecting tax is to issue land tax tickets according to the records in the book. (Payment of tax) Article 11: The land tax shall be sent to the Bureau by the taxpayer and paid in advance every six months. The taxpayer shall pay it within 15 days after receiving the land tax ticket stipulated in the above article. When paying the tax, a receipt shall be issued. The receipt shall be presented for inspection when there is an inquiry. Protest and supplementary collection methods Article 12: If the land tax ticket is inconsistent with the Bureau's resolution, or the land tax ticket is reissued, or there is a miscalculation, the taxpayer shall submit a written protest to the Bureau within 15 days after receiving the land tax ticket stipulated in Article 10. This protest shall not involve the resolution of the Board of Directors of this Bureau regarding the donation or the land price, nor shall it involve the land tax that has been approved and processed by the Board of Directors. Article 13: If the taxpayer does not receive a satisfactory reply one month after submitting a protest to the Bureau, he may file a lawsuit with the French Consulate Court. If the protest is considered to meet the conditions stipulated in Article 9 and is considered reasonable, the French Consulate Court may order the Bureau to return the overcharged amount. Article 14: If there is a shortfall in the land tax, the Bureau may reissue the land tax ticket to recover it within the scope stipulated in Article 12 before the final settlement. Article 15: If the taxpayer has applied for relief in accordance with the methods stipulated in Articles 12 and 13, or has exceeded the period for applying for relief, but delays in paying the land tax, the Bureau may sue for the arrears in the court of jurisdiction.

Wang Qingmu Sends a Telegram to President Jiang of the Executive Yuan Regarding the Jiangsu Railway

The Industry and Commerce News Agency said that Wang Qingmu telegraphed President Jiang of the Executive Yuan, Nanjing National Government Executive Yuan President Jiang Junjian, the railway in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, from Shanghai via Jiaxing and Hangzhou to Shaoxing and Ningbo, was approved by the Qing Dynasty in the late years for Jiangsu and Zhejiang to establish separate companies and promote commercial management. The Jiangsu section became only the section from Shanghai to Fengjing and the section from Qingjiang to Yangzhuang in Jiangbei. The Zhejiang section became only the section from Zhakou in Hangzhou to Gongchen Bridge. The section from Gen to Fengjing, connected to the Jiangsu Railway, and the section from Ningbo to Cao'e River in Shaoxing, have been opened to traffic one after another. In the second year of the Republic of China, the former Ministry of Transportation advocated nationalization, clarified the actual capital used by the two companies, and repaid it in 15 installments. Except for the 14 installments that have been repaid, the last installment has been delayed for many years. Recently, the Ministry of Railways reduced the compensation by half. According to the Jiangsu and Zhejiang commercial railways, it was difficult to operate, and the initial wish was not fulfilled. Only because the government changed its purpose and did not support the commercial road, the two companies let it go to the state in order to understand the intention of the department. It is not right to delay the repayment of the loan, how can it be reduced again? Most of the road construction in our country borrows foreign debts to repay the principal and interest, and there has never been a case of reduction. Why is it different for domestic debts? It is reported that the railway foreign debts have reached more than 100 million yuan, and the repayment of principal and interest costs tens of millions of yuan. Now the last installment of securities in Jiangsu and Zhejiang is reduced by half, saving only 800,000 yuan, while losing national credit, causing dissatisfaction among shareholders, and leaving the world ridiculed. The power of weight is very insignificant. It is proposed that the Executive Yuan order the Ministry of Railways to allocate funds to repay it to make up for the regret. In addition, the Zhejiang Road Liquidation Office announced that when the Zhejiang Road was nationalized, the department allocated a reward of 600,000 taels of silver, etc. According to this, the people of Jiangsu have never heard of it before. Now I see the announcement of the Zhejiang Liquidation Office. Jiangsu and Zhejiang are both commercially operated. Since it is called a reward, the affairs of Jiangsu and Zhejiang are the same, why does Zhejiang have it and Jiangsu does not? Railway engineering is heavy on bridges. Jiangsu has two huge bridges west of Songjiang, which have been standing for 30 years without any problems. Although the road line in Zhejiang is long, there are no such huge bridge projects from Fengjing to Hangzhou and from Ningbo to Cao'e River. If you really test and verify the results, the Jiangsu Railway should be better than the Zhejiang Railway, but why is the reward not as good? It is proposed that the Executive Yuan order the Ministry of Railways to check the old Ministry of Transportation files. When the Jiangsu and Zhejiang commercial roads were nationalized, there was a reward for Zhejiang and no reward for Jiangsu. What is the reason? Publish it clearly to show the people of the country. The former concerns national credit, and the latter belongs to partial weakness. Qingmu has been repeatedly questioned by shareholders, and forbearance and silence are not allowed by justice. He dares to forget his decay and rashly telegraph. He is anxiously waiting for orders. May you consider.

Rice Trade Association Held a General Meeting Yesterday, Broadcasting Market Prices on the Radio Every Day, Cracking Down on Radio Broadcasting and Price-Cutting Competition

The Municipal Rice Trade Association held a general meeting of members at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 1:00 pm yesterday after the authorities sent staff to reorganize it. More than 800 people attended. Mao Yun from the Municipal Party Department, Ye Weiyi from the Social Affairs Bureau, and Yuan Hongjun from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended and gave guidance. Qu Zhenhua, Zhang Nianxuan, Zhong Hongxun, Zhang Heming, Xia Xinzhai, and Pan Jibin served as the presidium. First, Qu Zhenhua reported the significance, followed by the party and government representatives' speeches. The results of the discussion were: (1) Cracking down on colleagues broadcasting on the radio. It was decided that the association would broadcast the market price on the radio every day. (2) Cracking down on colleagues using rubber roller rice milling machines. It was decided to pass it and hand it over to the Executive Committee for handling. (3) The association's creation of a newsletter. It was decided to publish a monthly magazine and start preparing it immediately. (4) Hiring a lawyer to provide services to members in case of suspicious cases. It was decided to pass it. (5) Cracking down on colleagues hanging up signs for false price-cutting competition. It was decided that the association would strictly crack down on it. Then, 15 executive committee members, 5 alternate members, 7 supervisory committee members, and 3 alternate members were elected. As a result of the election, Qu Zhenhua, Lu Wenshao, Zhang Nianxuan, Shi Hongxun, Zhang Heming, and Pan Jibin received the most votes and were elected as executive committee members. Qiang Zisheng, Chen Shaolian, Shu Zhanyuan, Huang Shuyu, and Jiang Qiusheng were elected as supervisory committee members. The full list will be announced today due to lack of time.

Overview of Silk Exports to the United States, Released by the International Trade Bureau

Our country's raw silk is mostly sold to the United States. Recently, due to the increasing exports of Japanese raw silk to the United States, the situation of Chinese silk in the main sales market is getting worse and worse. The report of the International Trade Bureau, the overview of our country's silk exports to the United States, is recorded as follows:

Silk Exports to the United States

Since 1924, Japanese silk has accounted for 81% of the total US raw silk imports. By 1934, it had increased to 98%. Since the US supply of raw silk has been completely monopolized by Japan, Chinese raw silk will inevitably be squeezed out by Japanese silk. However, most of China's raw silk is sold to the United States. Recently, only in 1929, the total amount of Chinese silk exported to the United States was 14,906,166 pounds, worth a total of 61,597,471 US dollars, which was a better situation. Otherwise, whether in quantity or value, it has become increasingly worse. The overview of exports to the United States in the past ten years is as follows: 1926, 10,249,690 pounds; 1927, 10,787,770 pounds; 1928, 10,527,407 pounds; 1929, 14,906,166 pounds; 1930, 9,880,811 pounds; 1931, 9,846,769 pounds; 1932, 2,530,494 pounds; 1933, 3,768,936 pounds; 1934, 1,102,573 pounds; 1934, 3,484,596 pounds. Among them, 1934 was the most declining, and last year has seen a recovery.

US Price Trend

Raw silk is the most expensive raw material in textiles, costing 70 cents to 1.70 US dollars per pound. Since the prevalence of rayon, although some silk fabrics can be replaced by rayon, there are still many fabrics that must use raw silk. The United States is the largest sales market for raw silk and rayon, and its market price fluctuations can also affect the whole world. In the past 15 years, the US silk price has changed greatly. For example, in 1919, it was worth 9.40 US dollars per pound. In 1929, it was reduced to 5.10 US dollars per pound. In 1934, the average price was only 1.30 US dollars per pound. At present, the silk price per pound is still only around 1.67 US dollars. The reason for the low price is mostly due to the fact that many textile industries in the United States have stopped work or reduced work, and the Japanese silk devaluation competition. However, in recent years, Japan has been actively reducing the cost of raw silk and government subsidies to maintain this monopoly trade.

Silk Transportation Method

Since the United States is the country with the most raw silk sales, the transportation method is very important in terms of the amount of freight. According to the research results of the National Textile Industry Alliance of the United States, 99% of the silk imported by the United States from the Far East is transported by land and sea, and only 1% is transported by water through the Panama Canal. In the future trend, the number of people gradually turning to water transportation is increasing year by year. By 1934, 90% was transported by water. The biggest blows suffered by Chinese silk exports are: (1) Fierce competition from Japanese silk; (2) Various weaknesses of Chinese silk itself. To remedy this, attention should be paid to centralizing capital and expanding production immediately; (3) Product standardization and quota standardization; (4) Reducing tariffs and encouraging exports. The above four points are the prerequisites for saving the silk industry. I hope that our government and industry and commerce will pay attention to it.

Suspension of Industrial Syndicate Organized by Various Banks

According to the New Voice News Agency, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and other banks, in order to thoroughly relieve industry and commerce, responded to the suggestions of various industries and planned to organize an industrial loan syndicate. After exchanging opinions among the banks, they believed that industrial loans were one of the businesses of each bank. Moreover, each bank had already handled them separately, such as mortgage loans for factories and goods. It seemed unnecessary to organize an industrial syndicate again. Therefore, the matter of planning to organize an industrial syndicate has already been suspended.

Request for Appropriation of Subsidies for Participation in the Texas Exposition: Wang Xiaolai and Others Telegraph the Ministry of Industry

Yesterday's News of Labor Strikes in Three British and American Factories

According to the Dagon News Agency, more than 2,600 male and female workers at the Third Factory of the British American Tobacco Company at 674 Huade Road and Tanpeng Road in Pudong went on strike on the morning of the day before yesterday in protest against the factory's suspension of female worker A Wu in the cigarette rolling department, and against the harsh treatment of workers by the Chinese manager Wei Ziqian, who did not allow them to take leave. Yesterday morning, male workers from various departments of the factory sent representatives Yao Ligen, Chen Jintang, Yang Xiangsheng, Yang Antai, female worker representative Zhu Acui, and employee representative Jiang Zhongheng, a total of six people, to meet with the foreign manager Huisi Xialuke at the factory to discuss solutions. Huisi replied that he would explain the reasons for the dismissal of female worker A Wu, and regarding the issue of Chinese manager Wei Ziqian not allowing workers to take leave, in the future, workers in various departments who need to take long leave for weddings, funerals, and celebrations will be allowed to apply for leave from the Western foremen in each department. If the Western foremen create difficulties, they should report to him personally, and leave will be granted. Although the workers expressed satisfaction with Huisi's response, they believed that Chinese manager Wei Ziqian must be dismissed immediately, otherwise, they would not be able to obtain the consent of all the workers, resulting in a stalemate for a long time without a solution. Currently, all the workers have decided to continue the strike and have requested assistance from the Fourth District Cigarette Workers' Union. Therefore, the labor strike is still difficult to resolve. All workers went to the factory as usual this morning, but did not work, it is said.

Bicycle Manufacturing Industry Association: Request to Change Freight Rates Approved

The Shanghai Bicycle Manufacturing Industry Association previously stated that fellow businesses operated vehicles and vehicle parts, which were transported and sold to other locations. For those transferred by railway, the railway bureau's regulations specified different grades, measured the weight, and used them as the standard for collecting freight. However, rubber tires have always been classified as second-class. As a result, parts such as pedals, brakes, and air pumps that have rubber products attached were all charged at the second-class rate by the railway bureau. Moreover, they could not be packed in the same box as third-class goods. Complicated situations often arose during inspections. The association had previously stated its reasons and sent a letter to the railway bureau requesting a change in the grade, changing rubber tires, pedals, brakes, air pumps, and items such as bicycle lights and locks to third-class for charging, in order to facilitate loading and transportation. A letter has now been received from the Vehicle Department of the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, which stated, "The case has been approved in accordance with your letter of June 3, regarding charging tree rubber products attached to bicycle parts, etc., at the third-class rate, etc." After reporting to the Ministry of Railways, the goods classification No. 20 order of July 31 stipulated, "Tree rubber tires for bicycles and bicycle lights, etc., are approved to be charged at the third-class rate, etc." Upon receiving this order, we should immediately comply and implement it. In addition to instructing the stations to comply, we are correspondingly replying to inform you, hoping that you will take note of it. The association has already notified fellow businesses to take note of it.

Child Drowns While Catching Crabs

At 2:00 p.m. on the day before yesterday, a group of children were catching crabs by the Huangpu River at the Xinkuan Wharf. Afterwards, they dispersed. A Chinese constable No. 2627 discovered a piece of clothing on the wharf and reported it to the Chief Constable's Office, which telephoned the Water Constable's Office and dispatched constable Qu Hehkui to investigate. Around dusk, when thunder rumbled and lightning flashed, the body of a young boy floated to the surface. The clothing belonged to the deceased. Constable Qu Hehkui immediately took the body to the South Wharf Lifesaving Bureau. After investigation, the constable summoned Bao Jinyou, a Ningbo native residing at 21 and a half Liangyi Lane, Yuezhou Road, to the scene. Bao Jinyou identified the deceased as his son, Bao Akang, who was 16 years old this year. Because his family was poor, he was eating free meals at the home of a relative who ran a canteen on Yong'an Street. Bao Jinyou stated that his son was swept into the river by a wave while catching crabs and drowned. The body was taken to the local court for a coroner's examination yesterday. Coroner Xie and his examining officer arrived at the scene to examine the body and confirmed the cause of death. The family was allowed to collect the body for burial.

No Cholera Found in This City: Announced by the Harbor Quarantine Office

The Harbor Quarantine Office of this port announced the status of infectious diseases in Shanghai Port for the week before midnight on the 15th of this month. The details are recorded below:

Last week, there were two cases of epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis among Chinese, with two deaths; eighteen cases of typhoid fever among Chinese and five among foreigners, with eleven deaths among Chinese; thirty-four cases of bacillary dysentery among Chinese and two among foreigners, with five deaths among Chinese and one among foreigners; six cases of diphtheria among Chinese; seven cases of scarlet fever among Chinese and two among foreigners. In total, sixty-seven Chinese and seven foreigners contracted infectious diseases, with twenty deaths among Chinese and two among foreigners. True cholera has still not been found in this port (other ports are also peaceful). Smallpox has also disappeared. However, the number of dysentery sufferers has increased sharply compared to last week, it is said.

Car Kills a Pregnant Woman: Driver Sentenced

A Ningbo woman, Zhang Ma, residing at 79 Tongle Lane, Huasheng Road, suddenly suffered from abdominal pain while pregnant. At 1:00 p.m. on the 17th, her husband, Zhang Junhong, hired a rickshaw driven by Wang Fuchang from Jiangbei, and the two sat together, intending to go to a doctor's office on Nanjing Road and Shilu Road for treatment. They were traveling from east to west on Dongxihua Road and Huaji Road when a No. 16621 truck from Tongchang Motor Transport Company of the South City 16th Wharf, driven by Wang Weiqing from Jiangbei, attempted to pass the rickshaw and accidentally overturned it. Zhang Junhong suffered a head injury, while his wife and the rickshaw driver Wang suffered minor injuries to their hands and feet. Chinese constable Ya Yonglu and Chinese constable No. 61 arrived at the scene after hearing the alarm and helped Zhang Junhong up. He was barely breathing and was sent to Tongren Hospital. He died at 9:35 p.m. that evening despite medical treatment. Ya Yonglu, a detective from the Huishan Police Station, took the body to the Philun Road Mortuary. The court dispatched a prosecutor to the mortuary to examine the body and then handed it over to his wife for burial. The truck driver, Wang Weiqing, was subsequently arrested by Ya Yonglu and detained in the police station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Special District Court. After questioning by Judge Dun Qing, he was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment.

300 Taels of Opium Seized En Route: Originally Intended for Transport to Another Location by Train: Zhang Huiqin Sentenced to Two Years of Imprisonment

Yesterday, a man surnamed Sun went to the Yuan Taichang Opium Shop in Nine Acres, Nanshi, and purchased ten packages of opium, weighing a total of 300 taels, instructing that they be delivered to the North Railway Station at approximately 2:00 p.m. the day before yesterday so that they could be transported to another location. The shop owner then instructed Zhang Huiqin, a Huzhou native who specialized in delivery, to place the opium in a suitcase, hire a rickshaw, and deliver it to the North Station to be handed over to Sun. However, when passing the intersection of Xizang Road and Guling Road, they were suddenly stopped by Chinese and Western detectives from the Xinzha Police Station. The detectives ordered Zhang to open the suitcase, but Zhang claimed that he did not have the key and could not open it. A constable then devised a method to open the suitcase and discovered that it was full of opium. They were all taken to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Criminal Division Eight of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the previous circumstances and prosecuted according to Article 5 of the Anti-Opium Regulations. When questioned, Zhang Huiqin admitted to transporting opium but claimed that each package only contained seven taels, for a total of 221 taels. Police lawyer Zhang Dayin stated that the opium all had a pagoda seal and was indeed 300 taels. After reviewing the testimony, Judge Tan Xinzhen sentenced Zhang Huiqin to two years of imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for three years for assisting others in transporting opium. The opium was confiscated.

Public Security Bureau of Caojiadu Sub-bureau Arrests Fierce Bandit: Foiled Before Robbery Attempt: Dared to Open Fire to Resist Arrest

The Caojiadu Sub-bureau of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau received a tip-off yesterday that several bandits were plotting to rob a wealthy family in the area. They immediately dispatched detectives to investigate in different directions. Sure enough, at approximately 1:00 p.m., they spotted six suspicious individuals in the Zhoujiaqiao area. They immediately followed them, but the bandits became aware of it and attempted to flee in different directions. Because the number of bandits was greater than the number of detectives, they could not split up. One of the bandit leaders dared to open fire to resist arrest. The detectives then joined forces to capture him on the spot. He was escorted back to the bureau. After questioning, it was learned that the bandit's name was Chen Zhixiang, a Jiangbei native, 31 years old, living in a thatched shed in Zhoujiaqiao. He used to work as a rickshaw puller. Because the bandit suffered a head injury when he resisted arrest, a letter was prepared after the interrogation and sent to the First Hospital of the Chinese Red Cross for diagnosis and treatment. After the hospital doctor cleaned and bandaged the wound, he was handed back to the escorts to continue the interrogation.

Another New Hurricane: But Distance is Very Far

According to the Central News Agency, hurricanes frequently occur in the South Pacific every summer and autumn, causing great harm to navigation as they come and go. After the hurricane that struck Hong Kong and Guangdong dissipated in western Yunnan, another hurricane has risen and is blowing towards the coasts of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Fujian. However, the distance is very far. At 6:00 a.m. yesterday, it had reached 135 degrees east longitude and 19 degrees north latitude. The hurricane center was 120 nautical miles, and the wind was moving very slowly and appeared to be stalling.

Opium Addict Commits Suicide in Prison Out of Fear of Punishment: Strangles Himself with a Sweatshirt Twisted into a Long Strip: Discovered and Sent to the Hospital, But Medical Treatment Was Too Late

Yang Changdang, a native of Anhui, 48 years old, worked as a worker at the Fufeng Qu powder factory on Moganshan Road. He was addicted to opium. On the 17th of this month, he went to Yanzi Nest at No. 405 Macau Road to smoke opium. He was discovered by the Putuo Road Police Station, which obtained a search warrant from the court and dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to secretly go to the location and arrest Li Xiaoyun, who ran the opium den, and four customers: Yang Changfu, Sun Bingcheng, and Tang Haizong. The next morning, they were escorted to the First Special Court. After interrogation, they were ordered to extend the detention. When the case was reviewed again yesterday morning, Yang and Li were selected to be detained at the police station, while Sun and Tang were allowed to post bail. However, at 12:15 p.m. yesterday, Yang, fearing punishment in the detention center, tore his sweatshirt into pieces, twisted them into a long strip, and hanged himself on the prison door. Chinese constable No. 2357, who was in charge of the prison, discovered it and quickly tried to untie him and administer artificial respiration. However, he was already barely alive and was sent to the police hospital. Medical treatment was ineffective, and he soon died. The body was taken to the Philun Road Mortuary. At approximately 10:00 a.m., Prosecutor Zhang Zongru from the First Special Court arrived at the mortuary to examine the body. According to Western patrol chief Hail, the police station's detention center had two rooms and a corridor. Recently, due to the hot weather, the prisoners were all sleeping in the corridor. Yang went to the detention room to hang himself after 12:00 p.m., so the other prisoners did not see him. Furthermore, according to Cheng Baoguo, he and the deceased were from the same hometown and were also colleagues. He was willing to collect the body for burial. After Zhang Zongru obtained the statement, he determined that the deceased, Yang Changfu, was male and had died by hanging himself. The body was handed over to Cheng Baoguo, a fellow villager, to collect and bury it after signing a pledge. It was also learned that the case had been concluded by Judge Tan Xinzhen in Criminal Division Eight of the court yesterday morning. The main text of the judgment was announced in court, stating that Li Xiaoyun was sentenced to seven months of imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for two years. Yang Changfu's part was not accepted. Sun Bingcheng and Tang Haizong were both found not guilty.

Navigation Bureau Facilitates Navigation: Lighted Buoys Installed at Lujiazui

In order to facilitate navigation, the Hydrographic Office has decided to install lighted buoys at Lujiazui, the Shanghai port of the Yangtze River Estuary. Its position is 100 degrees from the British Consulate flagpole, at a distance of 3.36 chains (each chain is equal to an Italian nautical mile), that is, 121 degrees 29 minutes east longitude and approximately 21 degrees 41 minutes north latitude. The light is a constant red. Lighted buoys will also be installed on the beach at Lujiazui. Its position is 119.5 degrees from the British Consulate flagpole, at a distance of 2.27 chains. The light is also a constant red.

Failure to Solicit Wireless Radio Advertisements Leads to Gang Extortion: Xu Langtian and Others Sentenced to Detention Separately

The "Urethra Pain Hospital" at No. 892 Edward Road specializes in treating venereal diseases and gonorrhea. The director of the hospital is Yu Luyi, a Mu native. In order to promote his business, he invited comedian He Shuangdai and others to broadcast advertisements on the Asia Sound Radio Station on Beile Road in the French Concession in May of this year. The broadcasts were later discontinued. Xu Langtian, a local comedian who specialized in broadcasting skits, 20 years old, residing at No. 517 Madrid, Gongguan Road, French Concession, went to the Urethra Pain Hospital to solicit the broadcast advertisement, but no deal was made. On the 10th of this month, Yu wanted to invite Xu Langtian to continue negotiations, but he did not have Xu's address. He inquired at the Asia Sound Radio Station, and the station informed Xu Langtian to go to the Urethra Pain Hospital for negotiations. Xu demanded a minimum broadcast fee of 70 yuan per month, but Yu only agreed to 30 yuan, so no deal was made again. Unexpectedly, on the 17th, Xu Langtian invited his companions Hu Zhisheng (who used to perform skits at the Great World) and others to suddenly go to the hospital and accuse Yu of repeatedly joking and causing him significant losses. They demanded compensation of 300 yuan, or at least 100 yuan. After negotiations, it was agreed on 45 yuan as reimbursement for losses, and Yu was forced to write a contract stating that the money would be paid on the 18th. On the 18th, Xu and others went to the Urethra Pain Hospital. Because Yu did not have the money to pay, he requested an extension of one day. Xu threatened that if the payment was delayed by one day, he would add 15 yuan. After Xu left, Yu felt that this situation was close to extortion and hired lawyer Fan Gang to report the situation to the Chengdu Road Police Station. The police station dispatched detective Zhu Yongjun to secretly wait at the Urethra Pain Hospital on the day before yesterday. Sure enough, Xu Langtian and Hu Zhisheng arrived, and when Yu handed over 60 yuan in banknotes, the detectives stepped forward to arrest them and confiscated the stolen money and the written agreement. They were taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, police lawyer Zhang Tianyin escorted them to Criminal Division Eight of the First Special Court and prosecuted them for extortion under Article 346, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. He also stated the details of the case. Furthermore, according to Yu Luyi's complaint, the hospital wanted to invite me to broadcast on the radio and directly contacted Zhu Wenhao, the runner at Asia Sound Radio Station, to sign a contract. Later, due to the price disagreement, no deal was made. Yu voluntarily reimbursed me for the loss of 60 yuan. There was no extortion. When questioned, Xu Langtian stated that the hospital wanted to invite me to broadcast on the radio and directly contacted Zhu Wenhao, the runner at Asia Sound Radio Station, to sign a contract. Later, due to the price disagreement, no deal was made. Yu voluntarily reimbursed me for the loss of 60 yuan. There was no extortion. When questioned, Hu Zhisheng said that Xu invited him to go, and he did not know anything else. Judge Tan Xinzhen reviewed the testimony and sentenced Xu Langtian to 14 days of detention for using violence and threats to force others to do something they had no obligation to do. Hu Zhisheng was sentenced to 7 days of detention for the same crime. The stolen 60 yuan was returned.

Public Concession Traffic Regulations: Implementation Temporarily Postponed

After the Public Concession's工部局 modified the traffic regulations, increasing restrictions on automobile parking in order to facilitate traffic, the automobile industry in this city strongly opposed it. Various Western newspapers have also commented on it. In order to show fairness, the 工部局 has agreed to give deep consideration to the points of debate, and because the board of directors is currently on summer vacation and the police chief is also away on vacation, in order to allow the board of directors and other important officials to discuss it, it has been decided to temporarily postpone the implementation date, which was originally scheduled to begin on September 5th. The date of implementation will be announced after the board of directors' vacation ends and considerable results have been considered. It is also reported that the new automobile parking regulations of the Public Concession 工部局 will be implemented soon. The Chinese Automobile Association believes that these regulations have many obstacles and has submitted a written opinion to the director and chief executive of the 工部局 the other day. The chairman of the association also made a personal presentation at that time, and then they discussed it with each other. After the discussion, the 工部局 claimed that it would consider the points raised and respond to the association within a reasonable period. The written opinion is very long, listing the inconveniences of the new regulations, especially for car owners who drive their own cars. Moreover, the automobile tax rate collected by the Shanghai Public Concession is quite high, and the 工部局 should allow automobiles to enjoy the current parking convenience, at least until suitable and free parking spaces are available. The new regulations have not been fully considered, so they should not be implemented immediately. Before making any changes, the current traffic situation must be thoroughly investigated, including parking. The development of automobile traffic will definitely increase day by day, and there is no possibility of reduction. Merely depriving car owners of the parking convenience they have enjoyed for many years cannot be resolved, so the entire vehicle traffic problem must be considered on a broad scale. Therefore, the 工部局's newly formulated parking regulations should be eased and allow various sectors to contribute their opinions, and then discuss a proper solution.

Lida Company: Details of Embezzlement Case

The case of the accountant of the Lida Radio Company at 395 Jing'an Temple Road being accused of embezzlement has been reported in this newspaper twice. It is now learned that the accountant, Yan Gongyin, is also a shareholder of the company and has been working as the accountant for five years, with a monthly salary of about 150 yuan. He usually works very hard and has been witnessed by his colleagues. When he resigned at the end of last month, he sent two letters to the authorities, describing the situation of the manager, Xi Shiying, embezzling more than 70,000 yuan during the reorganization of the company, and explaining the suffering of his resignation. At the same time, he sent a detailed list of the money and accounts he handled, along with the remaining amount of more than 110 yuan, all returned in full. Based on the above facts, the case of the accountant being accused of embezzling 5,000 yuan is obviously a matter of another background. According to those familiar with the inside story, Yan Gongyin stated when he resigned that the money he transferred was borrowed from the manager, Xi Shiying, personally and could be returned within one or two months, otherwise it would be used to recover the shares under his own name, and the rest would offset the special bonus that manager Xi Shiying had previously owed.

Ruling on Case Against Those Responsible for Tongyi Trust Company

The Tongyi Trust Company privately mortgaged or even sold off various government bonds deposited by depositors to other banks. This behavior was only exposed after the company went bankrupt on June 15. The general government bond depositors filed criminal self-accusations against all those responsible for the company, including the directors, supervisors, general managers, and assistant managers, requesting that they be prosecuted according to the crimes of embezzlement, fraud, and breach of trust in the criminal law, and the provisions of Article 230 of the Company Law, and filed a civil lawsuit requesting that the defendants be ordered to compensate for the losses. After repeated trials by the First Special District Local Court, except for the company's chairman Huang Suchu (Huang also served as general manager), managing director Liu Fangyuan, Xiong Muqu, director and manager Sun Xin Shen, directors Liu Ren, Wu Jingwen, and Chen Gongqia, seven people whose whereabouts are unknown and cannot be found, the trial was temporarily suspended, pending future arrest and handling. The remaining library manager Liu Zikang has been ordered to be detained, and assistant managers Zhou Longzhan, Jin Weiqin, and Deng Dongming have been ordered to be released on bail. The three directors, Xu Jilong, Zhou Shouliang, and Guo Yushang, and the two supervisors, Jiang Liuzhi and Chuan Zhuyin, were ordered to await public sentencing because they did not hold other positions in the company and the circumstances were lighter. At 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, the date for sentencing arrived. On the part of the plaintiffs, some were present in person, and some were represented by lawyers. Only Deng Dongming and Liu Zikang, who was in custody, were present as defendants, and the rest were absent. Soon after, Judge Zhong opened the court with the clerk and announced the verdict. Liu Zikang, Zhou Longzhan, Jin Weiqin, and Deng Dongming were found to have jointly and continuously embezzled other people's property, which constituted the crime of embezzlement. Each was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment and deprived of public rights for two years. Liu Zikang was returned to custody. Zhou, Jin, and Deng were released on their original bail during the appeal period. The remaining directors and supervisors were fined separately in accordance with the Company Law. The three directors, Xu Jilong, Zhou Shouliang, and Guo Yushang, jointly reported false information to the shareholders' meeting and were each fined 800 yuan. They jointly violated the Company Law by distributing dividends and were each fined 800 yuan. They should each execute a fine of 1,000 yuan. If they are converted to labor service, the amount calculated per day is determined by the ratio of 1,000 yuan to the number of days in six months. The remaining part is not penalized. Supervisors Jiang Yizhi and Chuan Zhuyin were also found to have reported false information to the shareholders' meeting and were each fined 600 yuan. They jointly violated the Company Law by distributing dividends and were fined 600 yuan. They should each execute a fine of 800 yuan. If they are converted to labor service, the amount calculated per day is determined by the ratio of 800 yuan to the number of days in six months. The remaining part is not guilty. The private lawsuit attached by the plaintiff was transferred to the Civil Division for review.

Correspondence

To the esteemed editor:

Regarding your newspaper's August 17th local news item, "Director Lu of the Shanghai Local Court Streamlines Operations," which stated that since Director Lu took office, he has reorganized important court affairs, and that among the personnel who submitted requests for transfer were civil court judges Sun Jikang, Chen Wukang, He Jingxian, etc., all of whom have been ordered by the Ministry to transfer to other locations. Attributing the transfer of judges to the director's streamlining of court affairs is, according to the facts, not entirely accurate. Upon investigation, before July 1st of this year, the Shanghai Local Court only had "Zheng Shikang" and no one named "Chen Wukang." "Zheng" and "Chen" are homophones, and the characters "Shi" and "Wu" are similar in shape, which may have caused the error. Shikang originally served as the president of the Yuyao County Court in Zhejiang. Last May, he was ordered to transfer to the Shanghai Local Court as a judge. He was diligent in handling cases and strict with himself. In the past year, no cases have been backlog, and he has not been negligent in his duties. Although he dares not boast of merit, he can claim to be blameless. This time, he was ordered by the Ministry to be assigned as a judge of the Fourth Branch of the Jiangsu High Court before Director Lu took office on June 30th (Director Lu took office on July 1st). Therefore, Shikang's transfer has nothing to do with Director Lu's streamlining of court affairs. Your newspaper's report that Director Lu submitted the transfer request is not factual. Such a report is related to personal reputation. Therefore, I am sending this special letter to your newspaper, requesting you to quickly correct it. Sincerely, Zheng Shikang, Judge of the Fourth Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, August 18th.

Shanghai's Film Industry

— Compiled by China Credit Information

(Shanghai Industry and Commerce Overview, No. 34)

According to Lianhua Film Company's estimates: In 1933, foreign films operating in China earned an average net profit of 40,000 yuan per film, totaling 16,840,000 yuan. According to the Shanghai Municipal Council's inspection statistics for the entire year of 1934, the number and proportion of foreign film imports were as follows:

Country Number Percentage

America 309 78

England 8 2

Japan 40 10

Other 40 10

This proves that the influence of foreign films is concentrated in Shanghai, especially American films. However, according to people in the foreign film business, business has declined significantly recently, partly due to increased taxes (estimated at 7 to 8 customs gold units per meter for customs duties, and 20 yuan for inspection fees per 500 meters sent to Beijing for inspection). On the other hand, due to the sluggish market, although theater ticket prices have fallen, they are not as full as before. Therefore, the income from showing a film is often insufficient to cover customs duties and transportation costs. The overall profit is estimated to be reduced by about 50% compared to previous years. (To be continued)

In addition, information about the supply of film, the manufacturing and sales of equipment, and temporary actor agencies are also included below.

Originally, only Kodak and Agfa sold film. Last year, Duepon Company was added. Among them, Agfa has the largest business, about 1 to 2 million yuan per year.

There are ten foreign companies selling equipment: Asian Electric Company, Reiss & Co., Music Electric Company, Loer Company, Peacock Company, Scientific Affairs Company, Western Electric Company, Cinema Supply Corp., jausou & Co., Star & Co., etc. Chinese manufacturers include Shanghai Company, Guangming Factory, Chuantong Company, China Wireless Research Institute, Dian Sheng Company, Shiqing Brothers Company, Hehe Company, Hengsheng Company, and eight others.

There are twelve temporary actor agencies: Shanghai Film Actors' Association, Xin, Hao You Company, Ming Guang, Ming Hua, Jin Hua, Xing Guang, Nan Yang, Jian Guo, Shi Dai Film Company, Hua Lun, Jian Hua, etc.

6. Current Situation of Shanghai's Cinemas

There are currently 34 cinemas in Shanghai. Only Jincheng shows first-run domestic films. Carlton, Guotai, Da Guangming, Lanxin, Nanjing, and Da Shanghai show first-run foreign films. Eleven theaters show second- and third-run domestic films, and sixteen theaters show second- and third-run foreign films. In terms of seating, first-run domestic films have 1,780 seats, first-run foreign films have 9,700 seats, second- and third-run domestic films have 10,636 seats, and second- and third-run foreign films have 15,750 seats. However, due to the limited supply of domestic films, each second- and third-run domestic film cinema still needs to show foreign films for several days each month. Even Jincheng, which shows first-run films, occasionally has this phenomenon.

Currently, first-run foreign film theaters charge 6 jiao per seat, second- and third-run theaters charge 2 jiao per seat; first-run domestic film theaters charge 5 jiao per seat, second- and third-run theaters charge 2 jiao per seat. If we calculate an average of 60% occupancy per show, the total annual ticket revenue for foreign films is 5,812,560 yuan, and the ticket revenue for domestic films is 1,954,800 yuan. But in reality, due to the insufficient supply of domestic films, first-run domestic film cinemas need to show foreign films for an average of six days per month. Based on this calculation, foreign film ticket revenue should increase to 6,203,520 yuan, and domestic film ticket revenue should decrease to 1,563,840 yuan. Domestic films only account for a quarter of foreign films. According to people in the theater industry, foreign films have only about 30% to 40% occupancy in recent years, while domestic films have an average of about 40% to 50% occupancy. Based on this estimate, the business of domestic films and foreign films in Shanghai in recent years is about 3 to 10. (To be continued)

(4)(2) Soccer and Basketball Schedule Arranged

The schedule has already been arranged. The matches for soccer and basketball will be determined by drawing lots. A total of sixteen countries will participate in soccer, using a knockout system. When we arrived in Munich, we received the news that we would face England in the first battle. England is the birthplace of soccer, so everyone was inevitably discouraged when this news came. Originally, only professional teams from England are formidable. The strength of the amateur team is also very mediocre. However, this time, six of the players on the English team were selected from an amateur team participating in the Scottish professional league. (English amateur teams can participate in professional leagues without violating amateur rules.) This amateur team ranked third in the league, so the English team participating in the conference is still very strong. Although our team is the leader of the Far East, I am afraid that we are still vulnerable. However, none of the players were discouraged. They firmly believed that there was not much difference in technical aspects. What they were worried about was the lack of physical strength. Therefore, they practiced long-distance running every day to cultivate endurance, in the hope of achieving some amazing results on the afternoon of August 6th. The overseas Chinese community has also prepared to support us and has reserved 300 tickets. In less than a day, they were sold out. It is expected that there will be a fierce battle on the day of the competition.

A total of twenty countries will participate in the basketball competition. The draw was held on the morning of the 27th. When eighteen countries had already drawn, there were five countries left: Japan, China, Mexico, Belgium, and the Philippines. The first to be drawn was Japan. When the second draw was in a woman's hand, the entire field became tense for a moment because the plastic skin was sealed so tightly that it could not be opened for a while. Everyone was chanting "China", "China". Finally, when it was opened, it was indeed China.

This scene was of great interest to the representatives of various countries and the people of Berlin, especially the fellow countrymen studying in Germany. The players' emotions were also very tense, preparing for a decisive battle on the afternoon of the first day. The basketball competition will use a double-round-robin system. Finally, six teams will be selected to compete for the championship. If we can defeat Japan in the first battle, according to the schedule, the future is very promising, and we will be able to get fourth or fifth place. If we fail, there is still a chance to improve. The entire schedule is too complicated, so it is omitted. Each match is limited to seven players, and it is stipulated that when changing players, the players who are replaced cannot re-enter the field. Therefore, the outcome of the match is very related to the coach's strategy and resourcefulness. Our lineup will not be officially decided until the day before the match.

(4)(3) Preliminary Victory for Basketball Friendly Match Against Peru

In order to explore strength and practice, the basketball team arranged two friendly matches before the start of the conference. Because the strength of European teams is too weak (Germany ranks third in Europe, but was defeated by Japan in a friendly match by 74 to 6), the American teams were scheduled. On the 29th, they played against South American Peru, and on the 31st, they played against the strongest team, the United States.

The friendly match against Peru was held at 3:30 pm on the 29th at the conference basketball court. Players from Japan, the Philippines, and the American basketball coach Tobin watched from the sidelines. There were also forty or fifty Chinese athletes and students who went to visit. The rest of the audience was turned away.

Before the match, everyone was worried about the results of this first battle after arriving in Europe. In the first half, we used our elite lineup to fight. Right forward Mou Zuoyun, center Wang Yuzeng, left forward Wang Hongbin, right guard Li Shaotang, and left guard Wang Nanzhen cooperated closely, which can be described as seamless. Attacking and defending were also very fast. After Mou Zuoyun opened the scoring with a free throw, he assisted Wang Yuzeng to score another goal. Since then, the momentum has grown stronger and stronger. Although the Peruvian team fought bravely, they had no power to fight back. At the end of twenty minutes, our team took a distant lead with 21 to 12.

In the second half, Coach Dong sent the second team to fight, so that everyone had the opportunity to play. In the beginning, we also took the lead all the way, creating a 12 to 6 advantage. But the Peruvian team fought back desperately and scored eight points in a row. In the second half, it was 12 to 14, and our team suffered a small setback. In total, it was 43 to 20, and our team initially gained prestige in Europe.

After the end, the reporter interviewed the American basketball coach Tobin and asked for his comments. Tobin said that the Chinese team has a very good foundation, is well-trained, and its skills can be described as excellent. But according to the Chinese team's style of play, it must have good referees when playing the match. Otherwise, it will definitely suffer a big loss. The reporter recalled the situation of the final with the Philippines at the last Far Eastern Games and admired Tobin's insights and sharp eyes, worthy of being a famous coach. Education News

Seventh Scientific Societies Joint Annual Meeting, Day Three: New Discoveries in Botany and Geography, Chiang Ying Discovers Two New Species of Chinese Apocynaceae, Yang Zhongjian Discovers New Species of Lystrosaurus and Chasmatosaurus

The Chinese Physiological Society Holds an Exhibition to Welcome the Seven Societies

(Special Dispatch from Peiping) The Joint Annual Meeting of the seven scientific societies—the Chinese Science Society, the Zoological Society, the Botanical Society, the Geographical Society, the Mathematical Society, the Physical Society, and the Chemical Society—held a paper presentation this morning (the 19th) at Peking University, with new discoveries made. In the afternoon, attendees visited the specimen exhibition of the Physiological Society. Details of the various aspects are recorded below.

New Discoveries in Botany

The Botanical Society held a paper presentation at 10:00 AM on the 19th at the Biology Classroom of Peking University. Chiang Ying read a paper on "A New Genus of Apocynaceae in Southeastern China." The new discoveries include the species Chunechites Tsiang and Chunechites Xylinabariopsoides Tsiang. These plants were collected from Zhejiang and Hainan. They are very similar to the genus Xylinabariopsis, but the ovaries of this genus have multiple ovules in each carpel, arranged in four rows, while Xylinabariopsis has only four ovules arranged in two rows. Regarding its nearly rotate corolla, it closely resembles Ehunecbites. The biggest difference is that each corolla lobe of the new genus Chunechites bears a tooth. A notable characteristic of Chunechites is its nearly wheel-shaped or nearly urn-shaped corolla with a very short corolla tube. Each very long and slightly sickle-shaped corolla lobe has small serrations on the edge. Its nectary disc is very short. In the subfamily Echtoideae, it is most similar to the genus Xylinabariopsia. This genus is dedicated to Professor Chen Huanyong, Chairman of the Chinese Botanical Society and Director of the Agricultural and Forestry Plant Research Institute of Zhongshan University.

New Discoveries in Geography

The Geographical Society held a paper presentation at 10:00 AM on the 19th in the [] Department of Peking University. Yang Zhongjian read "New Research on a Chinese Therapsid Fauna," discovering two [] animals. The results of his research are as follows: (1) Lystrosaurus hersi, a new species. Among the repaired specimens, this is the most complete. Besides the complete skull, most of the vertebrae, shoulder girdle, ischium, and almost all of the [] limbs are present. Some of the foot bones are missing. In the world, especially in [] fossils, such complete specimens are very rare. From the characteristics of its skull, such as the upward shift of the nostril position and the enlarged snout, it is known to be indeed a Lystrosaurus. Furthermore, by comparing it with known Lystrosaurus species, especially with the aforementioned Lystrosaurus mui, there are some differences. Therefore, we named it Lystrosaurus hersi, as a new species. (2) Another skeleton. Besides the complete specimen mentioned above, there is also a skeleton without a skull, but it undoubtedly belongs to the Dicynodontidae family. However, the most important parts of this skeleton, such as the [] girdle bone and ischium, are quite different from those of Lystrosaurus hersi. Therefore, I suspect that this skeleton may belong to the Xinjiang dicynodont, because the Xinjiang dicynodont only has a skull, and the new limbs are almost completely missing. The preservation condition and fossil color are also very similar. (3) Chasmatosaurus yuani, a new species. All the Xinjiang fossils mentioned above and previously recorded belong to the so-called Therapsida. Their living conditions were all near ponds, as relatively harmless omnivores. Another ferocious reptile coexisted with these animals at that time, often preying on young dicynodonts and therapsids. There is a so-called Chasmatosaurus in South Africa. Recently, similar animals have also been found in China, and their characteristics are quite similar.

Biological Nature of Protein

The Joint Annual Meeting held a public lecture at 10:00 AM on the 19th in the New Banquet Hall of Peking University. Wu Hsien spoke on the biological properties of protein, stating that we have known that protein is the main component of organisms for almost a hundred years, but chemists still do not fully understand the chemical structure of protein, so biologists cannot thoroughly understand the biological properties of protein. Protein is not only an important component of organisms but also a unique component of organisms. All organisms have protein, and all proteins come from organisms. Therefore, I believe that protein must have special properties, and these special properties are the basis of biological phenomena. From various studies, we know that the size of filterable viruses and bacteriophages is roughly comparable to protein molecules. Their diameters, in units of one millionth of a centimeter, are approximately as follows: (1) Bacteria, 20 to 100; (2) Filterable viruses, 25; (3) Enzymes, pepsin 4.5, sucrase 90; (4) Proteins, milk casein 8.3, egg protein 4.3; (5) Serum protein 7.9, hemoglobin []. Since filterable viruses and bacteriophages are roughly the size of protein molecules, their bodies cannot have many protein molecules, and they cannot have many other things besides protein. Looking at it this way, the difference between protein and organisms must not be far.

Physiological Specimen Exhibition

The Chinese Physiological Society and the private Peiping Union Medical College, to welcome the members of the Seven Scientific Societies Joint Annual Meeting, held a specimen exhibition at the Union Hospital this afternoon (the 19th). More than 300 members attended. The exhibition is described as follows: (1) Anatomy: Specimens of casts of various skeletal remains of the Peking Man, explained by Wei Jiaorui; Materials from embryology and several [], explained by Fu Taien. (2) Biochemistry: Vegetarian mice and [] mice, explained in detail by Wu Hsien. (3) []ology: A type of glass instrument for measuring hydrogen ion concentration (pH), explained by Chen Yuan. (4) Physiology: The sympathetic and parasympathetic nerve centers in the medulla oblongata and their connections, experiments conducted and explained separately by Lin Kesheng, Wang Shijun, Chen Meibo, and Yi Jianlong, using dogs as experimental subjects. The dogs were placed in the device for sympathetic nerve experiments, with a small amount of bleeding from the head, but they did not die. Heat production of muscles, explained by Feng Depi. (5) Glassware manufacturing: Various scientific glassware instruments, explained by Müller. (6) Internal Medicine: A continuous macerator for pregnant women's urine, the device is over ten feet high, storing a lot of pregnant women's urine, obtained from patients by the Department of Obstetrics and Gynecology of Union Hospital, exclusively for experimental use, explained by Chuan Swiss, Zhang Enlin. The method for measuring materials that promote estrus, also explained by Chuan. (7) Surgery: Urethral stones, foreign bodies in the respiratory tract, and other specimens, explained by Loukes. Specimens of penile squamous cell carcinoma are also displayed. Chinese men often suffer from this cancer due to phimosis. Circumcision is a preventive measure. (8) Radiology: Machines for manufacturing radium electrons and X-ray instruments, explained by Wang Runquan. (9) Pathology and Parasitology: Many pathological and parasitic specimens are displayed, explained by Hu Zhengxiang and Xu Liangjie. (10) Public Health: A demonstration of statistical machines, explained by Ms. Yuan Yijin et al. (11) Nursing: A demonstration of nursing techniques, practiced by Ms. Shan Xiewen et al. After visiting each department, refreshments were served at Building C, and the meeting adjourned at around 6 PM. (Jin)

Utilizing Chinese Plants

At the same time as the Joint Annual Meeting (4:00 PM), Hu Xiansu gave a public lecture on "How to Fully Utilize the Rich Resources of Chinese Plants" at Yenching's Bei Gong Lou. The main points are as follows: (1) Food: China has a vast territory, and there must still be excellent varieties of cereals that have not been propagated. If large-scale breeding and cross-breeding are carried out, unexpected harvests can be obtained. Yunnan wood beans are perennial plants that can be used to make tofu and other foods, but they cannot be used to extract oil. They should be widely planted. (2) Pasture grass: China has many pasture grasses, especially in the Northwest and Mongolia, with many drought-resistant species suitable for sand control and saline land growth. There must be many. (3) Lawn grass: China's provinces have different climates, and there are many types of lawn grass. Large-scale research should be carried out to facilitate landscape layout. (4) Legumes: This type of plant can increase nitrogen fertilizer in the soil. In addition to alfalfa and milk vetch used in farmland, there are many types that can be used. (5) Honey plants: This type of plant is closely related to beekeeping. A national survey should be conducted for reference by beekeepers. (6) Fruits: Wild fruits such as kiwifruit and raspberries should be cultivated. (7) Nuts: Nut cultivation is not common in China. Torreya, pearl chestnut, and hickory are the most precious, but few people plant them. Methods should be found to cultivate them. (8) Flowers: Chinese flowers are the best in the temperate zone, such as azaleas, primroses, and lilies, which are numerous and beautiful. Unfortunately, most have not been groomed. (9) Landscape trees: China has the most types of trees, especially those with landscape value. Modern cities and roadsides compete to use trees from the home country, which is more than sufficient. (10) Railroad ties: Coniferous trees such as Taiwania, [] pine, and larch are suitable. [] deciduous trees such as [] chestnut, birch, Chinese locust, [] cassia, [] toona, maple, hackberry, birch, [] elm, poplar, etc. China should conduct trials and choose the best ones to use. There is no shortage of materials. (11) Charcoal making: The materials used for charcoal cars are mainly hardwoods such as oak and [] that grow the most. Afforestation of this type of fuel wood is also a program that should be studied by silviculture. The tea oil tree produced in South China has the best branches for making charcoal. Widespread planting of tea oil trees can achieve two goals at once. (12) Paper making: China is rich in paper-making raw materials, such as rice straw, wheat straw, sugarcane bagasse, reeds, etc. Coniferous trees with low resin content, such as spruce, fir, bamboo, etc., are suitable for making paper by the sulfite method. Poplar and ailanthus are used for making paper by the soda method. (13) Artificial greening: Sugarcane can be used to make artificial greening. Other wood that can be used for paper making can also be used to make artificial greening. (14) Cellophane: The raw materials for making cellophane are the same as those for making artificial greening. (15) Wood distillation: Broad-leaved trees such as maple, oak, hickory, and birch are suitable. Distillation can yield calcium acetate, wood alcohol, and wood glue. Coniferous trees such as pine with pine branches are suitable. Distillation can yield turpentine, pine oil, and wood glue.

Science Society Business Meeting

The Chinese Science Society held a business meeting at Jingmu Lou at 2:00 PM. More than 30 people attended. Chairman Ren Hongjun reported on two points: 1. Discussion of proposals; 2. Deciding on the location of the next annual meeting. In addition, the Science Society held a board meeting in Peiping on the 16th and decided to establish a Science Medal to be awarded annually to those with excellent achievements. The medal is made of gold and is given in four categories: 1. Physics; 2. Biology; 3. Engineering; 4. Social Sciences. Next, the following motions were passed: 1. Motion to revise the current calendar, explained by Hu Dunfu. The current calendar is unevenly distributed, with unequal numbers of days in different months. Therefore, it must be fixed. This revision suggests that December and January each have 31 days, and the rest have 30 days. A year has 364 days, and the first day of each quarter is a Sunday. The day between the end of December and the beginning of January is called the End of Year Day. This decision is a resolution of the League of Nations and is scheduled to be implemented in 1939. We are submitting this motion, hoping that the government will prepare for implementation. After a long discussion, it was decided to first submit it to the remaining general assemblies for detailed discussion, and after it is passed by the General Assembly's Fellowship Meeting on the 20th, request it from the government. 2. Motion to decide on the location of the next annual meeting, resolution: (1) Wuhan; (2) Hangzhou, submitted to the General Assembly for decision. (Jin)

Inauguration of the Aurora University Library: Exhibition of French Books Opens

YMCA Vocational Night School News: Recruiting 150 Free Students

The Shanghai YMCA Vocational Night School has been established for more than 30 years. Now, in addition to reducing tuition fees, it has also specially set up 150 free places, so that those who are poor but of good character and learning and have aspirations will not regret it for the rest of their lives. As for the curriculum, it focuses on practical application, so that all graduates from the school can directly serve the society. Its structure is divided into primary and senior levels. The primary level focuses on English, and the senior level is divided into four departments: literature, commerce, accounting, and mathematics and science. A specialized course is also set up, and people from all walks of life, regardless of their level, can choose to study as they please. New students are currently being examined, and classes will begin on the 31st of this month.

Zhengzhong Bookstore Publishes: Junior High School Boy Scout Textbook

Since the Ministry of Education revised the middle school curriculum standards, junior high school boy scouts have been included in the regular courses, with two hours of instruction and one hour of practice per week. There were no suitable textbooks on the market. In view of the needs of school teaching, the bureau specially invited Chen Lifu et al. from the China Boy Scouts Association to edit a textbook for junior high school boy scouts. The teaching materials all follow the curriculum training standards issued by the China Boy Scouts Association, and the relevant parts of the specialized training that are needed by the times are selectively incorporated in order to adapt to the training during the national crisis. The whole book is in six volumes, one volume is taught per semester, for the six semesters of junior high school. The first and third volumes have now been published and shipped to Shanghai. It is heard that various schools have been purchasing them from the Shanghai distribution office of Zhengzhong Bookstore on Fourth Road.

Chiao Kuang Middle School: Chiao Kuang Middle School on Hart Road in this city has newly hired Ku Ke-ren, a graduate of Jiaotong University, to teach mathematics; Deng Hong-fu, a graduate of National Business College, to teach business subjects; Chiu Jui-chu, a graduate of Soochow Law School, to teach English; and Hsu An-ren, a graduate of Chung Kuo University and former teaching assistant at the school, to teach mathematics and physics.

The school has undergone a major internal reorganization, emphasizing practical mathematics and strict discipline. Classes began on the 20th of this month, and there are still openings in all grades. Ching Ru Elementary School: Ching Ru Elementary School, located on Huacheng Road across from the Slaughtering Company in the French Concession of this city, has always emphasized strict management and teaching. The school held its opening ceremony on the 20th of this month, with Principal Shen and the teachers addressing the new and returning students. Yesterday, over two hundred students attended. The school is still accepting new students, and the number of students arriving daily to register is quite crowded.

What You Need to Know About Asthma Treatment

— Shen Zhaoquan

Bronchial asthma, also known as asthma or phlegm asthma, and sometimes referred to as panting or dyspnea, is a disease caused by a specific respiratory difficulty resulting from the rigid spasm of the circular muscles of the small bronchioles. The symptoms usually occur suddenly at night, starting with chest tightness and a pale face, leading to a state of distress, profuse sweating, and very difficult breathing. It is labored, prolonged, and accompanied by wheezing, with abdominal muscles tense like a board. The coughed-up phlegm is yellowish-green.

(Treatment) When the disease occurs, administer three tablets of 'Holipin' (for adults), which can immediately stop the asthma and turn danger into safety. For radical cure and prevention of recurrence, continue taking it for one to two months to achieve full recovery. If one usually suffers from chronic bronchitis (i.e., persistent cough), their resistance to disease is certainly very weak, and the tissues are atrophied with declining physiological function, making it more difficult to cure. It is necessary to simultaneously take 'Phith Weal' to invigorate the physiological function of the lungs and strengthen lung power, so that the persistent cough is cured and there is no fear of asthma recurring.

(Diet and Care) Patients should avoid sudden changes in temperature and avoid irritating foods. They should breathe thin air and engage in outdoor exercise regularly. Patients who are physically weak, anemic, or have neurasthenia should also use nourishing tonics, such as 'Memory Neurotic' and 'Conbours's San-Vita-Cell,' to turn weakness into strength.

Commercial News

Finance: Pure Gold Plunges, Spot Gold Buying Suffers

The gold market saw a sharp drop of two pence in pure gold yesterday, with the standard price hanging at a small one dollar and thirty cents. Buying sentiment suffered a setback, falling back nine cents. The overall trend was erratic in the middle. Early in the morning, overseas telegrams indicated that the silver market was weaker in London and flat in the US. The forward silver price in Montreux fell by one to two cents. Exchange rates rose across the board. London spot gold fell by two pence. The central bank's pegged rates were announced, remaining flat in both the UK and the US. The customs gold unit fell by two cents. The standard gold price was listed, falling to 1123 yuan and 60 cents. Off-market preliminary trading opened, immediately falling to around 28 yuan. The morning opened with a low trading level, which then rose. Later, buying surged, temporarily exceeding demand. Lacking support from major players, it gradually declined. HSBC's pegged rates were announced, remaining flat in both the UK and the US. At this point, it stabilized slightly. Afterwards, major players re-entered, and although the silver balancing tax was reduced by half a cent, the spot buyers in the market gradually recovered, with some struggles in between. After entering, people's hearts were unsettled. Although the central bank was accepting cash, there were still many people selling off while prices were high. It flattened out around noon. The trend was erratic. Here is a record of the market situation in the first half of the day.

The morning opened at 1128 yuan and 10 cents, down seven cents from the previous close. Chunyuan Yong, Dada Cheng, and Natiao rose to 8 yuan and 30 cents. Yuanmao Yong, Fuxing Yong, Yicheng Yong, Yide Dada Cheng sold off, falling to 7 yuan and 30 cents. Shengyuan Yong took advantage of the low prices to buy in, and Dada Cheng came out and then re-entered, along with Futai Yong, Qianchang Xiang also bought, and although the silver balancing tax was reduced by half a cent, it still rose back to 8 yuan and 10 cents. Chunyuan Yong and Yicheng sold off, falling back to 7 yuan and 80 cents. Futai Heng, Qianchang Xiang, Dingkang Yuanmao Yong jointly bought, and rose again to 8 yuan and 40 cents. Yuanmao Yong suddenly came to sell off, and the noon close fell back to 1127 yuan and 90 cents.

The closing price, based on the central bank's standard gold price, fell to 1123 yuan and 60 cents. In terms of the closing price, it was raised by more than four yuan. The current month's registration is 1124 yuan, September is 1126 yuan, and October is 1128 yuan. The morning supplementary water is 1124 yuan. The price of pure gold is 1136 yuan and 10 cents. The spot market situation is stable. Tianjin goods are priced at 14 yuan more, but no transaction has been made. The price of 烚 red is 12 yuan more, and Shengyuan Yong bought 170 taels. The selling price is 15 yuan and a half more, but there are no buyers. Many parties for the forward are posting about two yuan, but no transaction has been made.

Trading in the market was flat. In summary, Qianchang Xiang, Tongfeng Heng, Futai Yong, Futai Heng, Dingkang, etc. were on the buying side, while Fuxing Yong, Chunyuan Yong, Tongtai Chang, Wanxing Shen, Dada Yong, Heng Yu, etc. were on the selling side. Yuanmao Yong first entered and then exited.

The market situation was uncertain in the first half of the day. The morning opening was 1128 yuan and 10 cents, and the noon close was 1127 yuan and 90 cents. The highest was 1128 yuan and 40 cents, and the lowest was 1127 yuan and 30 cents, a difference of 1 yuan and 10 cents. The result was a fall of nine cents from the previous close. Due to the recent accident involving the Yue-produced "Golden Mountain Twigs" on the *Xin Ning* steamer, with over 4,000 cases of goods destined for Shanghai lost, including 400 to 500 cases of glutinous rice twigs, the Shanghai market has suddenly tightened. "Lan Zhu" twigs from Zhangzhou have been scarce lately, leading to an upward trend. Yesterday, over a hundred cases opened, rising by about one yuan.
